### [32] [Beyond Mode Collapse: Distribution Matching for Diverse Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19461v1)
*Xiaozhe Li,Yang Li,Xinyu Fang,Shengyuan Ding,Peiji Li,Yongkang Chen,Yichuan Ma,Tianyi Lyu,Linyang Li,Dahua Lin,Qipeng Guo,Qingwen Liu,Kai Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: DMPO分布匹配优化解决RL模式坍塌，可迁移至agent RL训练

TL;DR: 提出DMPO，通过近似前向KL最小化实现分布匹配，有效防止on-policy RL中的模式坍塌，在组合优化、数学推理等任务上取得显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有on-policy强化学习方法（如GRPO）存在模式坍塌问题，即过早收敛到单一高奖励解，缺乏探索多样性，限制了性能。

Method: 提出DMPO，通过构建与轨迹奖励成比例的组级目标分布，并利用前向KL散度进行分布匹配，迫使策略覆盖多种模式，从而实现持续探索。

Result: 在NP-Bench上，DMPO质量比率提升9-12%（文本43.9% vs 40.1%，视觉43.1% vs 38.4%），在数学推理和领域外任务上分别提升2.0%和2.3%。

Conclusion: 分布匹配是一种实用且原则性的方法，能有效防止on-policy RL中的模式坍塌，通过保持多样性提升跨模态推理能力，并实现持续性能改善。

中文摘要：基于策略的强化学习方法（如GRPO）遭遇模式坍塌问题：它们表现出多样性的降低，一旦发现某个单一解便将概率质量集中于此，并停止探索其他策略。我们指出这源于反向KL最小化的模式寻求行为，该行为强化了找到的第一条高奖励轨迹，而不是维持多个不同解的分布。我们提出DMPO（分布匹配策略优化），通过对前向KL最小化的原理性近似来防止模式坍塌。DMPO构建一个组级别的目标分布，该分布与采样轨迹的奖励成比例，然后将策略分布与该目标对齐。这提供了模式覆盖行为，而无需从难以处理的全局目标分布中采样，从而在整个训练过程中实现持续探索。我们在NP难组合优化问题上验证DMPO，该问题存在指数级多的可行解，但只有少数接近最优解，是评估探索的理想测试平台。DMPO在基于文本的NP-Bench上达到了43.9%的质量比率（GRPO为40.1%），在基于视觉的NP-Bench上达到43.1%（GRPO为38.4%），分别相对提升了9%和12%。这些提升泛化到数学推理（+2.0%）和领域外任务（+2.3%），表明保持多样性的训练增强了跨模态的通用推理能力。我们的工作将分布匹配确立为一种实用且原则性的方法，用于防止基于策略的强化学习中的模式坍塌，一致的质量改进证明了在多种推理任务上的持续探索。

Original abstract: On-policy reinforcement learning methods like GRPO suffer from mode collapse: they exhibit reduced solution diversity, concentrating probability mass on a single solution once discovered and ceasing exploration of alternative strategies. We show this stems from reverse KL minimization's mode-seeking behavior, which reinforces the first high-reward trajectory found rather than maintaining a distribution over multiple diverse solutions. We propose DMPO (Distribution-Matching Policy Optimization), which prevents mode collapse through principled approximation of forward KL minimization. DMPO constructs a group level target distribution over sampled trajectories proportional to their rewards, then aligns the policy distribution to this target. This provides mode-covering behavior without requiring sampling from the intractable global target distribution, enabling sustained exploration throughout training. We validate DMPO on NP-hard combinatorial optimization, where exponentially many feasible solutions exist but only a few approach optimality, an ideal testbed for evaluating exploration. DMPO achieves 43.9% Quality Ratio on text-based NP-Bench (vs. GRPO's 40.1%) and 43.1% on vision-based NP-Bench (vs. 38.4%), demonstrating 9% and 12% relative improvements respectively. These gains generalize to mathematical reasoning (+2.0%) and out-of-domain tasks (+2.3%), showing that diversity-preserving training enhances general reasoning capabilities across modalities. Our work establishes distribution matching as a practical, principled approach to preventing mode collapse in on-policy RL, with consistent quality improvements demonstrating sustained exploration across diverse reasoning tasks.

</details>


### [33] [LC-ERD: Mining Latent Logic for Self-Evolving Reasoning via Consistency-Regulated Reward Decomposition](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24005v2)
*Yanyu Chen,Jiyue Jiang,Dianzhi Yu,Zheng Wu,Jiahong Liu,Jiaming Han,Xiao Guo,Jinhu Qi,Yu Li,Yifei Zhang,Irwin King*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LC-ERD自我演变推理框架，使用多智能体价值分解，通用agent改进方法

TL;DR: LC-ERD通过变分逻辑势和多智能体价值分解解决LLM自我对齐中的标签噪声、粗粒度监督和分布崩塌问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高质量过程数据稀缺，现有内生奖励自对齐面临三个挑战：模仿偏差导致标签噪声（奖励偏好统计似然而非逻辑真值）、粗粒度监督（全局奖励如GRPO无法提供步骤级指导）、分布崩塌（信号无法泛化且放大预训练偏差）。

Method: 提出LC-ERD框架，将自我对齐视为潜在结构挖掘：通过聚合模型潜在逻辑专长（LLE）的共识推导变分逻辑势以去噪推理流形，并基于IGM原则引入多智能体价值分解协议来量化单个步骤的效用。

Result: 实验表明LC-ERD提供稳健的自我进化路径，揭示了逻辑一致性与准确性之间的权衡，并识别出标准奖励遗漏的高价值推理模式。

Conclusion: LC-ERD有效解决了自对齐中的监督瓶颈，为LLM推理提供了更可靠的进化方向，代码已开源。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）推理的演进受到高质量过程数据稀缺的瓶颈制约。尽管通过内生奖励进行自我对齐提供了一种解决方案，但挖掘有效监督面临三个挑战：(1) 通过模仿偏差产生的标签噪声，奖励优先考虑统计可能性而非逻辑真值，造成“正确性幻觉”，掩盖了复合错误；(2) 粗粒度监督，稀疏的全局结果（例如在GRPO中）无法提供细粒度指导，将推理链视为一个整体；(3) 分布崩塌，信号无法泛化，且会放大预训练偏差。为了解决这些问题，我们引入了LC-ERD（逻辑一致内生奖励分解），一个将自我对齐视为潜在结构挖掘的框架。我们通过聚合模型潜在逻辑专长（LLE）的共识推导出一个变分逻辑势，以对推理流形进行去噪，并基于IGM原理引入一个多智能体价值分解协议来量化单个步骤的效用。实验表明，LC-ERD提供了一条稳健的自我进化路径，揭示了逻辑一致性与准确性之间的权衡，同时识别了标准奖励所遗漏的高价值推理模式。我们的代码可在 https://github.com/LC-ERD-repo/LC-ERD 获取。

Original abstract: The evolution of Large Language Model (LLM) reasoning is bottlenecked by the scarcity of high-quality process data. While self-alignment via endogenous rewards offers a solution, mining valid supervision faces three challenges: (1) Label Noise via Mimetic Bias, where rewards prioritize statistical likelihood over logical truth, creating a "correctness illusion" that masks compounding errors; (2) Coarse-Grained Supervision, where sparse global outcomes (e.g., in GRPO) fail to provide granular guidance, treating reasoning chains as monolithic; and (3) Distributional Collapse, where signals fail to generalize without amplifying pre-training biases. To address these, we introduce LC-ERD (Logic-Consistent Endogenous Reward Decomposition), a framework framing self-alignment as latent structure mining. We derive a Variational Logic Potential by aggregating consensus from the model's Latent Logic Expertise (LLE) to denoise the reasoning manifold, and introduce a Multi-Agent Value Decomposition protocol based on the IGM principle to quantify individual step utility. Experiments show LC-ERD delivers a robust self-evolution path, uncovering trade-offs between logic consistency and accuracy while identifying high-value reasoning patterns missed by standard rewards. Our code is available at https://github.com/LC-ERD-repo/LC-ERD.

</details>


### [34] [Beyond Fixed Budgets: Characterizing the Inelasticity and Limitations of Tree-of-Thought Reasoning Strategies](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20599v1)
*Atkia Mahila,Avinash Maurya,M. Mustafa Rafique,Bogdan Nicolae*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分析Tree-of-Thought搜索策略在不同预算下的行为，对agent规划方法有直接启发。

TL;DR: 评估了DPTS和SSDP两种ToT方法在不同计算预算、模型规模和问题难度下的表现，发现DPTS在低预算时冷启动慢，SSDP在高预算时前沿耗尽，提出需要自适应搜索策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索不同搜索策略在变化计算预算、模型规模和问题难度下的行为，以指导实际部署。

Method: 在Math500和GSM8K基准上，使用Llama-3B和Llama-8B模型，在3k-10k token预算下比较DPTS（蒙特卡洛树搜索）和SSDP（语义去重）两种ToT方法。

Result: DPTS低预算时因冷启动瓶颈表现差，高预算时扩展性好；SSDP高效达到候选解但前沿耗尽，无法进一步改进。

Conclusion: 固定探索或剪枝策略不足以应对计算连续体，需要能根据搜索进度和资源调整行为的自适应搜索策略。

中文摘要：思维树（Tree of Thought, ToT）搜索已成为提升大型语言模型推理能力的一个有前景的方向，但在实际部署这些方法时引发了一个鲜有系统关注的问题：不同的搜索策略在不同的计算预算、模型规模和问题难度下表现如何？在这项工作中，我们评估了两种具有代表性的ToT方法：基于蒙特卡洛树搜索的DPTS和基于语义去重的SSDP，在两个数学推理基准（Math500和GSM8K）、两种模型规模（Llama-3B和Llama-8B）以及四种token预算（3k-10k）上进行了实验。我们的分析揭示了这两种方法存在相互对立的局限性。DPTS在低预算时面临冷启动瓶颈：它需要充分的探索才能使其价值估计可靠，这使得它在资源受限的情况下表现不佳，尽管在高预算时具有强大的扩展行为。另一方面，SSDP能够高效地达到候选解决方案，但容易陷入前沿耗尽：其激进的节点合并永久地丢弃了未探索的路径，导致无论剩余预算多少都无法进一步改进。总之，这些发现表明，在计算连续体中，固定的探索策略或固定的剪枝策略都不足以应对。我们认为，有效的科学推理代理搜索需要能够根据搜索进度和可用资源调整其行为的策略。

Original abstract: Tree of Thought (ToT) search has become a promising direction for improving the reasoning capabilities of large language models, but deploying these methods in practice raises a question that has received little systematic attention: how do different search strategies behave under varying compute budgets, model sizes, and problem difficulties? In this work, we evaluate two representative ToT methods; DPTS, a Monte Carlo tree search based approach, and SSDP, a semantic deduplication based approach, across two mathematical reasoning benchmarks (Math500 and GSM8K), two model scales (Llama-3B and Llama-8B), and four token budgets (3k--10k). Our analysis reveals that the two methods exhibit limitations that pull in opposite directions. DPTS suffers from a cold-start bottleneck at low budgets: it requires sufficient exploration before its value estimates become reliable, making it a poor fit for resource-constrained settings despite strong scaling behavior at higher budgets. SSDP, on the other hand, reaches candidate solutions efficiently but is prone to frontier depletion; its aggressive node merging permanently discards unexplored paths, leaving it unable to improve regardless of how much budget remains. Together, these findings suggest that neither a fixed exploration strategy nor a fixed pruning strategy is sufficient across compute continuum. We argue that effective search for scientific reasoning agents requires strategies that can adapt their behavior based on search progress and available resources.

</details>


### [35] [Library Drift: Diagnosing and Fixing a Silent Failure Mode in Self-Evolving LLM Skill Libraries](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19576v2)
*Xing Zhang,Yanwei Cui,Guanghui Wang,Ziyuan Li,Wei Qiu,Bing Zhu,Peiyang He*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文识别并隔离了自进化技能库中的“库漂移”问题，提供了诊断方法和治理方案，显著提升了性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自进化技能库存在库漂移这一静默失败模式，导致性能停滞，且其机制未被理解。

Method: 提出可复现的触发条件（消融实验）、痕迹级诊断（证据日志）和已验证的修复方案（基于结果的淘汰、有界活跃容量、元技能创作先验）。

Result: 修复方案将MBPP+ hard-100上的留出pass@1从0.258提升至0.584（滚动增益+0.328）。

Conclusion: 八项消融实验揭示了治理机制的作用，为诊断和缓解任何自进化智能体中的库漂移提供了操作指南。

中文摘要：自进化技能库面临一种我们称之为“库漂移”的静默失败模式：无界技能积累缺乏基于结果的生命周期管理，导致检索退化、假阳性注入和性能停滞。最近的评估证实了该症状（大语言模型撰写的技能带来+0.0pp收益，而人工策划的技能带来+16.2pp（SkillsBench）），但潜在机制尚未被隔离。我们提供：（1）一个**可复现的触发条件**：隔离漂移的消融实验——一个禁用技能注入（平坦基线，+0.002），一个施加过早淘汰（主动伤害，-0.019）；（2）**痕迹级诊断**：一个仅追加的证据日志，包含每技能的贡献分数、归因判定和路由器参与度指标，使失败在影响最终任务分数之前可见；（3）**一个经过验证的修复方案**：一个最小的治理方案（基于结果的淘汰 + 有界活跃容量 + 元技能创作先验），将MBPP+ hard-100上100轮中的留出pass@1从0.258基线提升到晚期窗口平均值0.584（滚动增益+0.328）。八项消融实验分解了哪些治理机制是承重的，哪些是被包含的，为诊断任何自进化智能体中的库漂移提供了具体操作指南。

Original abstract: Self-evolving skill libraries face a silent failure mode we term \emph{library drift}: unbounded skill accumulation without outcome-driven lifecycle management causes retrieval degradation, false-positive injections, and performance stagnation. Recent evaluation confirms the symptom (LLM-authored skills deliver +0.0pp gain while human-curated ones deliver +16.2pp (SkillsBench)), yet the underlying mechanism has not been isolated. We provide (1) a \textbf{reproducible trigger}: ablations that isolate drift: one disables skill injection (flat floor, +0.002), one imposes premature retirement (active harm, $-$0.019); (2) \textbf{trace-level diagnostics}: an append-only evidence log with per-skill contribution scores, attribution verdicts, and router engagement metrics that make the failure visible before it reaches end-task scores; and (3) a \textbf{verified fix}: a minimal governance recipe (outcome-driven retirement + bounded active-cap + meta-skill authoring prior) that lifts held-out pass@1 from a 0.258 baseline to a late-window mean of 0.584 (rolling gain $+$0.328) on MBPP+ hard-100 over 100 rounds. Eight ablations decompose which governance mechanisms are load-bearing and which are subsumed, providing a concrete playbook for diagnosing library drift in any self-evolving agent.

</details>


### [36] [SceneCode: Executable World Programs for Editable Indoor Scenes with Articulated Objects](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19587v1)
*Puyi Wang,Yuhao Wang,Linjie Li,Zhengyuan Yang,Kevin Qinghong Lin,Yangguang Li,Yu Cheng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 使用agentic backbone和代码生成创建可交互场景，与coding agent高度相关。

TL;DR: SceneCode通过将自然语言提示编译为可执行的代码驱动世界，实现了从静态网格到物理可交互室内场景的程序化生成，提升了场景保真度和资产可交互性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有室内场景合成方法将生成内容表示为静态网格，仅从策划资产库继承关节，限制了对象级可控性和按需生成新可交互资产的能力。

Method: 提出SceneCode框架，包含房间级智能体骨干（规划器-设计器-评判器循环）生成布局和资产请求，采用五种代码生成策略将请求转换为Blender Python程序，并通过执行引导的修复与细化循环验证，最终编译为SDF物理仿真资产，由持久化场景状态注册表链接各组件。

Result: SceneCode在场景级合成、对象级资产质量、人类判断和下游机器人交互上优于基线，生成更符合提示的室内场景、更干净的网格结构和可加载的关节元数据。

Conclusion: 可执行世界程序能有效生成物理可交互的室内场景，提升资产质量和仿真兼容性，为具身AI和机器人操作提供更实用的场景合成方案。

中文摘要：室内场景合成支撑着具身人工智能、机器人操作和基于仿真的策略评估，其中有用的场景不仅需要指定环境的外观，还需要指定其对象的结构。然而，现有的流水线通常将生成的内容表示为静态网格，并仅从策划的资产库中继承关节，这限制了对象级别的可控性，并阻止按需生成新的可交互资产。我们通过将物理可交互的室内场景合公式化为程序化世界生成来解决这一差距，并提出了SceneCode，这是一个将自然语言提示编译为可执行的、代码驱动的室内世界而非不透明网格集合的框架。一个房间级别的智能体骨干首先将提示转化为结构化的房屋布局，并通过规划器-设计器-评判器循环发出每个对象的资产请求。然后每个请求被路由到五个代码生成策略之一，并转换为合成的逐部分Blender Python程序，这些程序通过执行引导的修复与细化循环进行验证。得到的程序被编译为可用于仿真的资产，并导出为用于物理模拟的SDF。一个持久化场景状态注册表将对象请求、可执行程序、渲染几何体和仿真资产链接起来，将场景组装转变为可追踪和局部可编辑的世界构建过程。我们在场景级合成、对象级资产质量、人类判断和下游机器人交互方面评估了SceneCode。结果表明，可执行的世界程序改进了符合提示的室内场景生成，并生成了具有更干净网格结构和仿真器可加载的关节元数据的资产。项目页面：https://scene-code.github.io/。

Original abstract: Indoor scene synthesis underpins embodied AI, robotic manipulation, and simulation-based policy evaluation, where a useful scene must specify not only what the environment looks like, but also how its objects are structured. Existing pipelines, however, typically represent generated content as static meshes and inherit articulation only from curated asset libraries, which limits object-level controllability and prevents new interactable assets from being produced on demand. We address this gap by formulating physically interactable indoor scene synthesis as programmatic world generation, and present SceneCode, a framework that compiles a natural language prompt into an executable, code-driven indoor world rather than a collection of opaque meshes. A room-level agentic backbone first turns the prompt into a structured house layout and emits per-object AssetRequests through a planner--designer--critic loop. Each request is then routed to one of five code-generation strategies and converted into a synthesized part-wise Blender Python programs that are validated through an execution-guided repair-and-refine loop. The resulting programs are compiled into simulation-ready assets, and exported as SDF for physics simulation. A persistent scene-state registry links object requests, executable programs, rendered geometry, and simulation assets, turning scene assembly into a traceable and locally editable world-building process. We evaluate SceneCode across scene-level synthesis, object-level asset quality, human judgment, and downstream robot interaction. Results show that executable world programs improve prompt-faithful indoor scene generation and produce assets with cleaner mesh structure, and simulator-loadable articulation metadata. Project page: https://scene-code.github.io/.

### [37] [Formal Skill: Programmable Runtime Skills for Efficient and Accurate LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19604v1)
*Xi Zhang,Meijun Gao,Yuntian Zhao,Xinyu Tan,Yilun Yao,Feiyu Wang,Yanshu Wang,Dingsiyi,Tong Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出Formal Skill抽象和运行时，直接面向LLM agent的可靠执行和工具使用。

TL;DR: 提出形式化技能（Formal Skill）抽象，通过可执行状态机和钩子策略替代冗长提示，实现令牌高效且可强制执行的智能体控制，并在FairyClaw运行时中实现，在Harness-Bench上以更少令牌取得优异平均分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能主要分为两类：一是非正式的Markdown技能和指令包，将过程编码为长自然语言文档，令牌效率低且难以强制执行；二是函数调用、MCP服务器和框架工具，虽结构化单个动作，但将工作流状态、策略执行和完成纪律置于技能之外，导致控制不完整。

Method: 引入形式化技能（Formal Skill）作为运行时原生抽象，包含JSON元数据和动作模式、Python执行器、钩子控制逻辑、路由和技能本地运行时状态。在FairyClaw开源事件驱动运行时中实现，将可重用过程从提示文本迁移到可执行状态机和钩子策略。

Result: 在Harness-Bench评估中，FairyClaw相比基线方法显著减少令牌使用量，同时获得极具竞争力的平均分，特别在对形式化技能依赖较强的任务上表现突出。

Conclusion: 形式化技能提供了一种令牌高效且可强制执行的技能抽象，FairyClaw作为其实现，验证了该方法在提升智能体控制效率和效果方面的有效性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）智能体越来越多地在真实工作空间中运行，其中工具和技能决定了模型推理是否能转化为可靠行动。现有的技能大多是非正式的：Markdown技能和指令包将过程编码为冗长的自然语言文档，而函数调用、模型上下文协议（MCP）服务器和框架工具则结构化单个动作，但通常将工作流状态、策略执行和完成纪律留在技能本身之外。我们引入了形式化技能（Formal Skill），这是一种运行时原生抽象，通过JSON元数据和动作模式、可靠的Python执行器、钩子控制的逻辑、形式化技能路由以及技能本地运行时状态来表示可重用的能力。通过将可重用过程从重复的提示文本移动到可执行的状态机和钩子策略中，形式化技能为智能体提供了一个令牌高效且可强制执行的控界面。我们在FairyClaw中实现了这一抽象，这是一个开源的事件驱动运行时，用于可执行、可观察和可组合的形式化技能。在Harness-Bench上，FairyClaw在显著减少令牌使用量的同时获得了极具竞争力的平均分数，在那些凸显形式化技能作用的任务上表现尤为出色。

Original abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) agents increasingly act inside real workspaces, where tools and skills determine whether model reasoning becomes reliable action. Existing skills remain largely informal: Markdown skills and instruction packs encode procedures as long natural-language documents, while function calling, Model Context Protocol (MCP) servers, and framework tools structure individual actions but usually leave workflow state, policy enforcement, and completion discipline outside the skill itself. We introduce Formal Skill, a runtime-native abstraction that represents reusable capability with JSON metadata and action schemas, reliable Python executors, hook-governed control logic, Formal Skill routing, and skill-local runtime state. By moving reusable procedure from repeated prompt text into executable state machines and hook policies, Formal Skill gives agents a token-efficient and enforceable control surface. We implement the abstraction in FairyClaw, an open-source event-driven runtime for executable, observable, and composable Formal Skills. On Harness-Bench, FairyClaw obtains highly competitive average scores while using substantially fewer tokens, with especially strong results on tasks that expose the role of Formal Skill.

### [38] [Pseudocode-Guided Structured Reasoning for Automating Reliable Inference in Vision-Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19663v1)
*Weicong Ni,Tianbao Jiang,Linlin Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出伪代码引导的结构化推理框架，可启发agent规划策略选择。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出PStar框架，包括抽象推理函数、结构化伪代码库和难度特征向量（DFV），自适应选择推理路径。

Result: 在POPE上达87.1%，MMStar上达68.0%，超越GPT-4V，显著降低幻觉率。

中文摘要：视觉-语言模型（VLM）正在成为机器人自动化高级推理的基石，使机器人能够解析自然语言命令并感知其环境。然而，它们对幻觉的敏感性在决策中引入了关键性失败，在物理部署中带来了重大的安全性和可靠性风险。现实世界任务的开放性加剧了这一挑战，因为问题在难度和模态上差异巨大，需要稳健且适应性强的推理策略。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了伪代码引导的结构化推理框架（PStar），它自适应地选择结构化伪代码推理路径，以帮助VLM进行灵活且逐步的推理。我们首先设计了一组抽象推理函数，并制定了结构化伪代码库来表示模块化推理策略。关键的是，我们设计了一个难度特征向量（DFV），允许模型评估问题复杂度并自适应地选择合适的推理策略——增强了鲁棒性和可解释性。大量实验表明，PStar显著降低了幻觉率，在POPE上达到了87.1%的最高分，在MMStar上达到了68.0%，甚至超过了GPT-4V。通过提供一种经过验证的减少视觉-语言错误的机制，PStar为在现实世界自动化系统中部署更可信赖和确定性的VLM迈出了关键一步，在这种系统中，此类错误可能导致灾难性后果。

Original abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) are becoming the cornerstone of high-level reasoning for robotic automation, enabling robots to parse natural language commands and perceive their environments. However, their susceptibility to hallucinations introduces critical failures in decision-making, posing significant safety and reliability risks in physical deployments. This challenge is exacerbated by the open-ended nature of real-world tasks, where questions vary vastly in difficulty and modality, demanding robust and adaptable reasoning strategies. To tackle this, we propose the Pseudocode-guided Structured Reasoning framework (PStar), which adaptively selects structured pseudocode reasoning paths to help VLMs perform flexible and step-by-step reasoning. We first design a set of abstract reasoning functions and formulate a structured pseudocode library to represent modular reasoning strategies. Crucially, we design a Difficulty Feature Vector (DFV) that allows the model to assess question complexity and adaptively choose appropriate reasoning strategies-enhancing robustness and interpretability. Extensive experiments demonstrate that PStar significantly reduces hallucination rates, achieving state-of-the-art scores of 87.1% on POPE and 68.0% on MMStar, outperforming even GPT-4V. By providing a validated mechanism to reduce visual-language errors, PStar offers a critical step toward deploying more trustworthy and deterministic VLMs for real-world automated systems, where such errors can lead to catastrophic outcomes.

### [39] [EngiAI: A Multi-Agent Framework and Benchmark Suite for LLM-Driven Engineering Design](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19743v2)
*Gioele Molinari,Florian Felten,Soheyl Massoudi,Mark Fuge*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计包含工作流、RAG和HPC三个评估维度的基准套件，并构建基于LangGraph的多智能体系统EngiAI作为参考实现，通过七个专门智能体的监督架构协调任务。

Conclusion: 提出的基准和参考实现能有效评估多智能体系统，揭示条件分支和长工作流是主要挑战，开源模型虽落后但代际进步明显。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）智能体越来越多地应用于工程设计任务，但现有的评估框架未能充分涵盖结合模拟、检索和制造准备的多智能体系统。我们引入了一个包含三个评估维度的基准套件：（1）一个工作流基准，具有七种针对不同认知需求的提示风格——包括直接工具使用、语义消歧、条件分支和工作记忆任务；（2）一个检索增强生成（RAG）基准，通过门控评分隔离检索对参数选择的贡献；（3）一个高性能计算（HPC）基准，评估SLURM集群上端到端ML训练编排。除了基准测试外，我们还提出了EngiAI，一个基于LangGraph的多智能体系统（MAS）参考实现，通过协调七个专门智能体的监督架构来操作基准测试，统一拓扑优化、文档检索、HPC作业编排和3D打印机控制。在四个LLM后端和两个EngiBench问题上，专有模型在Beams2D上实现了96-97%的平均任务完成率，而开源4B参数模型达到了55-78%，并显示出明显的代际改进。条件分支最具挑战性，在Photonics2D上条件风格的任务完成率降至20-53%。RAG门控确认了检索增强得分接近完美（约1.0），而无检索时接近零，验证了评估设计。在HPC编排上，一个模型在100%的运行中完成了所有流水线步骤，而另一个降至50%，表明多步骤指令遵循在长时间工作流中会退化。

Original abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) agents are increasingly applied to engineering design tasks, yet existing evaluation frameworks do not adequately address multi-agent systems that combine simulation, retrieval, and manufacturing preparation. We introduce a benchmark suite with three evaluation dimensions: (1) a workflow benchmark with seven prompt styles targeting distinct cognitive demands-including direct tool use, semantic disambiguation, conditional branching, and working-memory tasks; (2) a Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) benchmark with gated scoring isolating retrieval contributions to parameter selection; and (3) an High Performance Computing (HPC) benchmark evaluating end-to-end ML training orchestration on a SLURM cluster. Alongside the benchmark we present EngiAI, a Multi-Agent System (MAS) reference implementation built on LangGraph that operationalizes the benchmark by coordinating seven specialized agents through a supervisor architecture, unifying topology optimization, document retrieval, HPC job orchestration, and 3D printer control. Across four LLM backends and two EngiBench problems, proprietary models achieve 96-97% average task completion on Beams2D, while open-source 4B-parameter models reach 55-78%, with clear generational improvement. Conditional branching proves most challenging, with task completion dropping to 20-53% for the conditional style on Photonics2D. RAG gating confirms near-perfect retrieval-augmented scores (about 1.0) versus near-zero without retrieval, validating the evaluation design. On HPC orchestration, one model completes all pipeline steps in 100% of runs while another drops to 50%, revealing that multi-step instruction following degrades over long-running workflows.

### [40] [Memory-Augmented Reinforcement Learning Agent for CAD Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19748v1)

Original abstract: Automatic generation of computer-aided design (CAD) models is a core technology for enabling intelligence in advanced manufacturing. Existing generation methods based on large language models (LLMs) often fall short when handling complex CAD models characterized by long operation sequences, diverse operation types, and strong geometric constraints, primarily because reasoning chains break and effective error-correction mechanisms are lacking. To address this problem, this paper proposes a memory-augmented reinforcement learning framework for CAD generation agents. The framework encapsulates the underlying geometric kernel into a structured toolchain callable by the agent and builds a closed-loop mechanism of design intent understanding, global planning, execution, and multi-dimensional verification. It also designs a dual-track memory module consisting of a case library and a skill library, and proposes a dynamic utility retrieval algorithm. By introducing reinforcement learning into retrieval and policy optimization, the agent can effectively avoid retrieval traps in which examples are semantically similar but geometrically infeasible, enabling online self-correction and continual evolution without additional large-scale annotated data. Experiments show that the proposed method significantly improves both the success rate and geometric consistency on complex CAD model generation tasks.

### [41] [OpenComputer: Verifiable Software Worlds for Computer-Use Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19769v1)
*Jinbiao Wei,Qianran Ma,Yilun Zhao,Xiao Zhou,Kangqi Ni,Guo Gan,Arman Cohan*

Motivation: 现有计算机智能体评估缺乏可验证性和细粒度状态检查，需要构建可靠且可审计的测试环境。

Method: 提出OpenComputer框架，包含四个组件：app-specific状态验证器、自进化验证层、任务生成管道和评估平台，覆盖33个桌面应用和1000个任务。

Result: OpenComputer的硬编码验证器与人类裁决高度一致，优于LLM作为裁判的评估；前沿智能体在端到端任务上表现不佳，开源模型性能下降明显。

Conclusion: OpenComputer提供了可验证的软件世界，凸显了当前计算机智能体在鲁棒自动化方面的持续差距，验证器可靠性优于LLM评估。

中文摘要：我们提出了OpenComputer，一个基于验证器的框架，用于为计算机智能体构建可验证的软件世界。OpenComputer集成了四个组件：（1）应用特定的状态验证器，通过真实应用暴露结构化检查端点；（2）自进化验证层，利用执行反馈提高验证器可靠性；（3）任务生成流程，合成真实且可机器检查的桌面任务；（4）评估平台，记录完整轨迹并计算可审计的部分信用奖励。在当前形式下，OpenComputer涵盖33个桌面应用和1000个最终任务，涉及浏览器、办公工具、创意软件、开发环境、文件管理器和通信应用。实验表明，OpenComputer的硬编码验证器比LLM作为裁判的评估更接近人类裁决，尤其是在成功取决于细粒度应用状态时。前沿智能体在端到端完成方面仍然困难，尽管有部分进展，开源模型从其OSWorld-Verified分数出现急剧下降，暴露出鲁棒计算机自动化的持续差距。

Original abstract: We present OpenComputer, a verifier-grounded framework for constructing verifiable software worlds for computer-use agents. OpenComputer integrates four components: (1) app-specific state verifiers that expose structured inspection endpoints over real applications, (2) a self-evolving verification layer that improves verifier reliability using execution-grounded feedback, (3) a task-generation pipeline that synthesizes realistic and machine-checkable desktop tasks, and (4) an evaluation harness that records full trajectories and computes auditable partial-credit rewards. In its current form, OpenComputer covers 33 desktop applications and 1,000 finalized tasks spanning browsers, office tools, creative software, development environments, file managers, and communication applications. Experiments show that OpenComputer's hard-coded verifiers align more closely with human adjudication than LLM-as-judge evaluation, especially when success depends on fine-grained application state. Frontier agents struggle with end-to-end completion despite partial progress, and open-source models exhibit sharp drops from their OSWorld-Verified scores, exposing a persistent gap in robust computer automation.

### [42] [Distribution-Free Uncertainty Quantification for Continuous AI Agent Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19779v1)
*Yuxuan Gao,Megan Wang,Yi Ling Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: AI agent评估的不确定性量化，通用方法，对agent可靠性评测有价值。

TL;DR: 将分裂保形预测和自适应保形推断应用于连续AI智能体评估，实现了无分布覆盖保证，并开发了多智能体管道的不确定性界限和保形弃权规则，实验验证了方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为连续AI智能体评估提供无分布假设的覆盖保证，并处理多智能体管道中的不确定性、排名中的错误控制以及大规模多重检验问题。

Method: 采用分裂保形预测和自适应保形推断（ACI）生成预测区间；通过模拟验证组合不确定性界限；提出用于成对排名的保形弃权规则和FDR校正弃权；使用18个实时信号每小时评估50个智能体。

Result: 保形区间在24小时标定误差低于0.02；ACI在智能体发布后区间扩大35%后重新收敛；条件覆盖率平均值80.4%，90%智能体在[72%,90%]；情感分歧预测排名不稳定性（r=0.64）；循环性控制验证捕获额外信号（ρ_s=0.52）。

Conclusion: 所提框架在连续AI智能体评估中提供可靠的分布自由覆盖保证，有效处理多智能体场景的不确定性和多重检验，并通过实验验证其有效性。

中文摘要：我们将分裂保形预测和自适应保形推断（ACI）适应于连续AI智能体评估，为预测的质量分数提供无分布覆盖保证。保形区间在24小时范围内所有名义水平上的标定误差低于0.02，而ACI在智能体发布后正确地将区间扩大35%，然后重新收敛。我们进一步开发了多智能体管道的组合不确定性界限（通过跨阶段相关性ρ在[-0.5, 0.9]范围内的模拟验证）、用于成对排名的保形弃权规则（具有受控的误排率）以及用于排行榜规模多重检验的FDR校正弃权。通过每小时收集的18个实时信号评估50个智能体，我们显示每个智能体的条件覆盖率很好地集中在名义水平附近（平均值80.4%，90%的智能体在[72%, 90%]范围内），并且跨源情感分歧预测了排名不稳定性（r=0.64, p<0.01）。循环性控制的验证确认了该框架捕获了超出基准的信号（ρ_s=0.52, p<0.01, n=35）。代码和数据根据CC BY 4.0发布。

Original abstract: We adapt split conformal prediction and adaptive conformal inference (ACI) to continuous AI agent evaluation, providing distribution-free coverage guarantees for forecasted quality scores. Conformal intervals achieve calibration error below 0.02 across all nominal levels at the 24h horizon, while ACI correctly widens intervals by 35% following agent releases then reconverges. We further develop compositional uncertainty bounds for multi-agent pipelines (validated via simulation across inter-stage correlations rho in [-0.5, 0.9]), a conformal abstention rule for pairwise rankings with controlled false-ranking rate, and FDR-corrected abstention for leaderboard-scale multiple testing. Evaluating 50 agents via 18 real-time signals collected hourly, we show that per-agent conditional coverage is well-concentrated around the nominal level (mean 80.4%, 90% of agents within [72%, 90%]), and that cross-source sentiment divergence predicts ranking instability (r=0.64, p<0.01). A circularity-controlled validation confirms the framework captures signal beyond benchmarks (rho_s=0.52, p<0.01, n=35). Code and data are released under CC BY 4.0.

### [43] [Prior Knowledge or Search? A Study of LLM Agents in Hardware-Aware Code Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19782v1)
*Dmitry Redko,Albert Fazlyev,Konstantin Sozykin,Maria Ivanova,Evgeny Burnaev,Egor Shvetsov*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: LLM在代码优化中主要依赖预训练先验，而非反馈或代理结构，实验显示其在不同场景下表现各异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估LLM在代码优化任务中各个组件的贡献以及探索失败的机制，因为现代LLM代理结构复杂，难以直接分析。

Method: 通过三个受控实验：纯黑盒优化、零样本内核生成和反馈循环内核优化，分析LLM的行为。

Result: LLM在纯黑盒优化中是贪婪的；零样本内核生成对输入大小不敏感且性能随罕见大小下降；反馈循环中CUDA提升而TVM IR下降。

Conclusion: LLM在代码优化中高度依赖预训练先验，而非反馈或代理结构，语言密度影响优化效果。

中文摘要：LLM发现与优化系统越来越多地应用于各个领域，它们实现了一种常见的提议-评估-修改循环。这种优化或发现过程通过对来自环境的反馈进行上下文条件化来推进。然而，随着现代LLM代理在结构上越来越复杂，评估哪些组件贡献最大，以及这种探索何时以及如何可能失败变得困难。我们通过三个受控实验来回答这些问题。我们的发现：（1）在纯黑盒优化中，LLM表现为贪婪优化器。（2）在零样本内核生成中，提供明确的输入大小信息没有可测量的效果，模型会收敛到相同的内核参数，无论大小或温度如何，就好像大小指令不可见一样。此外，当任务是为不常见的内核大小执行内核优化时，无论使用哪种语言，性能都会急剧下降。（3）在反馈循环内核优化中，CUDA在迭代反馈下单调改进，而TVM IR则主动退化，这表明当模型使用低密度语言时，内核优化会退化。我们的结果得出结论，在代码优化任务中，LLM高度依赖于预训练的先验知识，而不是提供的反馈或代理结构。

Original abstract: LLM discovery and optimization systems are increasingly applied across domains, implementing a common propose-evaluate-revise loop. Such optimization or discovery progresses via context conditioning on received feedback from an environment. However, as modern LLM agents are increasingly complex in their structure, it is difficult to evaluate which components contribute the most, and when and how this exploration may fail. We answer these questions through three controlled experiments. Our findings: (1) In pure black-box optimization, LLMs act as greedy optimizers. (2) In zero-shot kernel generation, providing explicit input-size information has no measurable effect, models converge to the same kernel parameters regardless of size or temperature, as though the size instruction were invisible. Moreover, when tasked to perform kernel optimization for uncommon kernel sizes, performance sharply degrades regardless of the language used. (3) In feedback-loop kernel optimization, CUDA improves monotonically under iterative feedback, while TVM IR actively degrades, which demonstrates that kernel optimization degrades when models operate with low-density language. Our results conclude that LLMs in code optimization tasks highly depend on pretrained priors rather than provided feedback or agentic structure.

### [44] [From Prompts to Pavement Through Time: Temporal Grounding in Agentic Scene-to-Plan Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19824v1)
*Ahmed Y. Gado,Omar Y. Goba,Alaa Hassanein,Catherine M. Elias,Ahmed Hussein*

Selection reason: 多agent场景规划，提出时间条件化架构，可迁移至coding agent的时序推理。

TL;DR: 本文研究了自动驾驶中智能体间通信的时间条件化对推理连贯性的影响，发现虽然时间条件化改变了推理风格，但没有显著提高标准NLP指标，但定性分析显示其有助于危险预测和策略性行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM/LMM在自动驾驶场景理解中缺乏时间基础，导致连续动作推理不一致，危害安全性和可解释性。

Method: 提出三种逐步增加时间整合的规划器架构，在BDD-X数据集子集上使用语义、句法和逻辑指标评估。

Result: 时间条件化未带来标准NLP正确性指标的显著提升，但定性分析发现其能产生预测性危险推理、稳定纠正行为和策略性分歧。

Conclusion: 基于提示的时间基础存在局限性，本研究为时间场景到规划推理建立了第一个实证基准。

中文摘要：最近尝试使用大型语言模型（LLMs）和大型多模态模型（LMMs）集成来支持自动驾驶车辆（AVs）的高级场景解释和规划时，仍然将时间视为次要属性。这种时间基础的缺乏导致了对连续动作推理的不一致，损害了安全性和可解释性。本研究探讨了智能体间通信中的时间条件化能否在不损害语义或逻辑一致性的情况下保持或增强连贯性。为此，我们引入了三种逐步增加时间整合的规划器架构，并在BDD-X数据集的精选子集上使用语义、句法和逻辑指标进行评估。结果表明，虽然时间条件化重塑了推理风格，但在基于标准NLP的正确性指标上并未产生统计显著的改进。然而，定性分析揭示了哨兵（Sentinel）中的预测性危险推理、稳定的纠正行为和策略性分歧。这些发现阐明了基于提示的时间基础的局限性，并为时间场景到规划推理建立了首个实证基准。

Original abstract: Recent attempts to support high-level scene interpretation and planning in Autonomous Vehicles (AVs) using ensembles of Large Language Models (LLMs) and Large Multimodal Models (LMMs) continue to treat time as a secondary property. This lack of temporal grounding leads to inconsistencies in reasoning about continuous actions, undermining both safety and interpretability. This work explores whether temporal conditioning within inter-agent communication can preserve or enhance coherence without introducing degradation in semantic or logical consistency. To investigate this, we introduce three planner architectures with progressively increasing temporal integration and evaluate them on curated subsets of the BDD-X dataset using semantic, syntactic, and logical metrics. Results show that while temporal conditioning reshapes reasoning style, it yields no statistically significant improvements in standard NLP-based correctness metrics. However, qualitative analysis reveals predictive hazard reasoning, stable corrective behavior, and strategic divergence in the Sentinel. These findings clarify the limits of prompt-based temporal grounding and establish the first empirical benchmark for temporal scene-to-plan reasoning.

### [45] [Streamlined Constraint Reasoning via CNN Pattern Recognition on Enumerated Solutions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19895v1)
*Patrick Spracklen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM驱动约束推理流线，结合CNN模式识别，可视为自动优化agent方法

TL;DR: 提出一种结合CNN和LLM的新方法，通过枚举解并训练CNN检测结构模式，再让LLM生成流线型约束，在多个问题上获得巨大加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动流线型方法要么基于语法搜索要么直接对模型文本提示LLM，缺乏对解的结构观察。本文动机是利用解的结构信息来引导LLM生成更好的流线型。

Method: 枚举可行解，对比学习训练CNN区分解与非解，提取判别信号，用LLM生成候选MiniZinc流线型约束。

Result: 在三个强化基准模型上，流水线大幅减少时间，最佳单一流线型加速比达932x、356x、1103x。

Conclusion: 表明基于解结构学习的流线型生成方法有效，能发现超越传统强化的约束。

中文摘要：约束编程从业者通过按风险顺序应用分层技术来加速困难问题。首先应用标准强化（对称性破坏和隐含约束），它保持可满足性。流线型约束将搜索限制在解的结构子族中，不保持可满足性，并作为最后的杠杆保留。现有的自动流线型综合方法要么搜索约束语法，要么直接对问题模型提示大型语言模型。我们提出了一种不同的方法：枚举可行解，对比性地训练卷积神经网络对抗扰动非解以检测结构模式，并通过LLM驱动的综合将CNN的判别信号转化为候选的MiniZinc流线型。CNN将LLM的约束生成锚定在观察到的解结构上，而不仅仅是模型文本。我们在强化基准模型上进行了评估，其中流线型发现是剩余的性能杠杆。我们的流水线在强化Vessel Loading上实现了98.8%的时间缩减，在强化Social Golfers上实现了98.6%，在Black Hole上实现了89.4%，最佳单一流线型分别达到了几何平均加速比932倍、356倍和1103倍。发现的流线型包括Vessel Loading上的基于类的打包约束，Social Golfers上的超越强化的规范形式，以及Black Hole上的布局坐标边界。

Original abstract: Constraint programming practitioners accelerate hard problems through a layered set of techniques applied in order of risk. Standard hardening (symmetry-breaking and implied constraints) is applied first and preserves satisfiability. Streamliner constraints, which restrict search to a structural sub-family of solutions, do not preserve satisfiability and are reserved as a final lever. Existing automated streamliner-synthesis approaches either search a constraint grammar or prompt a Large Language Model directly on the problem model. We propose a different approach: enumerate feasible solutions, train a Convolutional Neural Network contrastively against perturbed non-solutions to detect structural patterns, and translate the CNN's discriminative signal into candidate MiniZinc streamliners through LLM-driven synthesis. The CNN grounds the LLM's constraint generation in observed solution structure rather than model text alone. We evaluate on hardened benchmark models where streamliner discovery is the residual performance lever. Our pipeline achieves 98.8% portfolio time reduction on hardened Vessel Loading, 98.6% on hardened Social Golfers, and 89.4% on Black Hole, with best-single streamliners reaching geometric-mean speedups of 932x, 356x, and 1103x respectively. Discovered streamliners include class-based packing constraints on Vessel Loading, beyond-hardening canonicalisations on Social Golfers, and layout-coordinate bounds on Black Hole.

</details>


### [46] [PEEK: Context Map as an Orientation Cache for Long-Context LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19932v1)
*Zhuohan Gu,Qizheng Zhang,Omar Khattab,Samuel Madden*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 长上下文LLM agent的上下文地图缓存系统，对coding agent记忆重用有直接启发

TL;DR: PEEK通过维护一个可动态更新的上下文地图作为持久提示，显著提升了LLM代理在重复长上下文任务中的准确性和效率，并降低了成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法缺乏对重复上下文中可重用方向性知识的维护，导致代理在不同调用中无法有效利用上下文结构，效率低下。

Method: 提出PEEK系统，包含Distiller（提取知识）、Cartographer（转化为结构化编辑）和Evictor（基于优先级控制令牌预算）三个模块，在代理提示中维护一个固定大小的上下文地图。

Result: 在长上下文推理和信息聚合任务上，PEEK比强基线提升6.3-34.0%，迭代次数减少93-145次，成本比ACE低1.7-5.8倍；在上下文学习上，解决率和评分准确率分别提升6.0-14.0%和7.8-12.1%，成本比ACE低1.4倍。

Conclusion: 上下文地图作为一种持久提示机制，能有效帮助LLM代理更准确、高效地与重复外部上下文交互，并具有良好的泛化性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）代理越来越多地在长且重复的外部上下文（如文档语料库和代码仓库）中运行。在多次调用中，现有方法要么保留代理的轨迹、对原始材料的被动访问，要么保留任务级策略。它们都没有保留我们认为对重复相同上下文工作负载最需要的东西：关于重复上下文本身的可重用方向性知识（例如，上下文包含什么、如何组织，以及历史上哪些实体、常量和模式是有用的）。我们引入了PEEK，一个系统，它缓存并维护这些方向性知识作为上下文地图：代理提示中的一个小的、恒定大小的工件，使其能够持久地窥视外部上下文。该地图由一个可编程缓存策略维护，该策略包含三个模块：一个Distiller，从推理时信号中提取可转移知识；一个Cartographer，将其转化为结构化编辑；以及一个基于优先级的Evictor，强制执行固定的令牌预算。在长上下文推理和信息聚合方面，PEEK比强基线提高了6.3-34.0%，同时使用93-145次更少的迭代，并且成本比最先进的提示学习框架ACE低1.7-5.8倍。在上下文学习方面，PEEK分别将解决率和评分准确率提高了6.0-14.0%和7.8-12.1%，成本比ACE低1.4倍。这些增益在LM和代理架构中普遍适用，包括OpenAI Codex（一个生产级编码代理）。总之，这些结果表明，上下文地图帮助长上下文LLM代理更准确、更高效地与重复的外部上下文交互。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents increasingly operate over long and recurring external contexts, like document corpora and code repositories. Across invocations, existing approaches preserve either the agent's trajectory, passive access to raw material, or task-level strategies. None of them preserves what we argue is most needed for repeated same-context workloads: reusable orientation knowledge (e.g., what the context contains, how it is organized, and which entities, constants, and schemas have historically been useful) about the recurring context itself. We introduce PEEK, a system that caches and maintains this orientation knowledge as a context map: a small, constant-sized artifact in the agent's prompt that gives it a persistent peek into the external context. The map is maintained by a programmable cache policy with three modules: a Distiller that extracts transferable knowledge from inference-time signals, a Cartographer that translates it into structured edits, and a priority-based Evictor that enforces a fixed token budget. On long-context reasoning and information aggregation, PEEK improves over strong baselines by 6.3-34.0% while using 93-145 fewer iterations and incurring 1.7-5.8x lower cost than the state-of-the-art prompt-learning framework, ACE. On context learning, PEEK improves solving rate and rubric accuracy by 6.0-14.0% and 7.8-12.1%, respectively, at 1.4x lower cost than ACE. These gains generalize across LMs and agent architectures, including OpenAI Codex, a production-grade coding agent. Together, these results show that a context map helps long-context LLM agents interact with recurring external contexts more accurately and efficiently.

</details>


### [47] [Robotics-Inspired Guardrails for Foundation Models in Socially Sensitive Domains](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19940v1)
*Rebecca Ramnauth,Drazen Brscic,Brian Scassellati*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 机器人启发的运行时防护栏框架，可迁移至agent行为控制

TL;DR: 提出Grounded Observer框架，将护栏问题重新定义为交互轨迹的运行时行为控制，在三个敏感领域实现有效干预。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有护栏方法仅提供经验性风险降低，缺乏可执行的行为保障，且局限于单个输出而非交互轨迹，需要更严格的运行时控制。

Method: 借鉴机器人学中的形式化构造，将护栏建模为在不确定闭环系统中对交互轨迹的运行时约束执行，并实例化为Grounded Observer框架。

Result: 在闲聊、家庭自闭症治疗和学校行为降级三个真实场景中，该框架实现了运行时干预，有效减轻了向不良交互状态的漂移，并能适应多样化社会背景。

Conclusion: 框架具有扩展潜力，未来工作应朝向更强保障的研究方向推进。

中文摘要：基础模型正越来越多地部署在教育、心理健康和护理等社会敏感领域，在这些领域中，失败往往是累积性的且依赖于上下文。现有的护栏方法——从训练时对齐到提示、解码约束和事后审核——主要提供经验性风险降低而非可执行的行为保障，并且很大程度上将安全性视为单个输出的属性而非交互轨迹。我们将护栏重新定义为对交互轨迹的运行时行为控制问题，借鉴机器人学引入用于在不确定的闭环系统中执行约束的形式化构造。我们在Grounded Observer（有根基的观察者）框架中实例化这些思想，并将其应用于三个真实世界部署场景：闲聊、家庭自闭症治疗和学校的行为降级。在这些场景中，该框架能够在适应不同社会背景的同时实现运行时干预，以减轻漂移到不良交互状态的风险。我们讨论了该框架的扩展，并提出了朝向更强保障的研究方向。

Original abstract: Foundation models are increasingly deployed in socially sensitive domains such as education, mental health, and caregiving, where failures are often cumulative and context-dependent. Existing guardrail approaches -- ranging from training-time alignment to prompting, decoding constraints, and post-hoc moderation -- primarily provide empirical risk reduction rather than enforceable behavioral guarantees, and largely treat safety as a property of individual outputs rather than interaction trajectories. We reframe guardrails as a problem of runtime behavioral control over interaction trajectories, drawing on robotics to introduce formal constructs for constraint enforcement in uncertain, closed-loop systems. We instantiate these ideas in the Grounded Observer framework and apply it across three real-world deployments: small talk, in-home autism therapy, and behavioral de-escalation in schools. Across settings, the framework enables runtime interventions that mitigate drift into undesirable interaction regimes while adapting to diverse social contexts. We discuss extensions to the framework and propose research directions toward stronger guarantees.

### [48] [Probabilistic Tiny Recursive Model](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19943v1)
*Amin Sghaier,Ali Parviz,Alexia Jolicoeur-Martineau*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 概率小递归模型用于推理时计算扩展，可增强agent规划能力

TL;DR: PTRM通过在TRM递归中注入高斯噪声实现随机探索，无需重新训练，在多个推理任务上大幅提升准确率且参数极少。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: TRM的确定性递归会收敛到次优解且缺乏逃逸机制。

Method: 在每个递归步注入高斯噪声，并行运行多条轨迹，利用Q头选择最佳答案。

Result: Sudoku-Extreme准确率从87.4%提升至98.75%，Pencil Puzzle Bench从62.6%提升至91.2%，优于LLM（91.2% vs 55.1%）且成本极低。

Conclusion: PTRM是一种有效的测试时计算扩展方法，无需任务特定调整，即可显著提升推理性能。

中文摘要：小循环模型(TRM)通过迭代精炼潜在状态和最终答案，以现代大型语言模型(LLM)参数的一小部分解决复杂推理任务。虽然强大，但其确定性递归可能导致收敛到次优解，且无逃逸机制。常见的解决方法是依赖测试时特定任务的输入扰动，并结合投票进行答案聚合。我们引入概率性TRM (PTRM)，这是一个与任务无关的测试时计算扩展框架，通过随机探索解决这一局限。PTRM在每个深度递归步骤注入高斯噪声，使并行轨迹能够探索不同的解盆地，并使用模型现有的Q头（用于原始TRM中的早停）进行选择。无需重新训练或任务特定增强，PTRM在基准测试中实现了显著的准确率提升，包括Sudoku-Extreme（87.4%到98.75%）和来自Pencil Puzzle Bench的各种谜题（62.6%到91.2%）。在后者上，PTRM的准确率几乎是前沿LLM的两倍（91.2%对比55.1%），成本不到其0.0001倍，仅使用7M参数。

Original abstract: Tiny Recursive Models (TRM) solve complex reasoning tasks with a fraction of the parameters of modern large language models (LLMs) by iteratively refining a latent state and final answer. While powerful, their deterministic recursion can lead to convergence at suboptimal solutions, without escape mechanism. A common workaround relies on task-specific input perturbations at test time combined with answer aggregation via voting. We introduce Probabilistic TRM (PTRM), a task-agnostic framework for test-time compute scaling that addresses this limitation through stochastic exploration. PTRM injects Gaussian noise at each deep recursion step, enabling parallel trajectories to explore diverse solution basins, and selects among them using the model's existing Q head (used for early stopping in the original TRM). Without requiring retraining or task-specific augmentations, PTRM enables substantial accuracy gains across benchmarks, including Sudoku-Extreme (87.4% to 98.75%) and on various puzzles from Pencil Puzzle Bench (62.6% to 91.2%). On the latter, PTRM achieves nearly double the accuracy of frontier LLMs (91.2% vs. 55.1%) at less than 0.0001x the cost, using only 7M parameters.

</details>


### [49] [GeoX: Mastering Geospatial Reasoning Through Self-Play and Verifiable Rewards](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20006v1)
*Kyeongjin Ahn,Seungeon Lee,Krishna P. Gummadi,Meeyoung Cha*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自对弈框架结合可验证奖励，通用agent训练机制，可迁移。

TL;DR: GeoX通过自我博弈框架利用可执行程序和验证器，无需大规模标注数据即可提升地理空间推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有地理空间推理依赖大量人工标注数据，成本高昂且难以覆盖组合性问题空间，因此需要一种无需大规模标注数据的方法。

Method: GeoX框架采用单一多模态策略，将空间问题作为可执行程序提出，并在溯因、演绎和归纳三种模式下求解，通过验证器执行程序产生奖励信号，利用强化学习优化策略。

Result: GeoX在多个基准上持续提升基础VLM平均最高5.5个点，达到或超过使用数百万标注数据训练的基线。

Conclusion: GeoX展示了自我博弈框架在地理空间推理中的有效性，并提供了一个通过自我博弈积累的基准，有望推动该领域发展。

中文摘要：地理空间推理需要解决场景复杂空间结构上的图像基础问题。然而，由于标注庞大且组合性强的问题空间成本高昂，这一能力的发展受到阻碍。我们提出了GeoX，一个自我博弈框架，通过可执行程序获取空间逻辑，这些程序产生可验证的奖励，不依赖于大规模人工标注数据。给定卫星或航空图像，我们的框架采用单一的多模态策略，将空间问题提议为可执行程序，并在三种推理模式——溯因、演绎和归纳——下解决这些问题，涉及空间基元和图像理解工具。验证器执行每个程序以将奖励信号转化，通过强化学习联合优化两个角色。GeoX持续提升其基础VLM平均最多5.5个点，匹配或超越基于数百万标注数据训练的常规基线。伴随提出的方法，我们发布了一个通过自我博弈积累的地理空间理解基准。

Original abstract: Geospatial reasoning requires solving image-grounded problems over the complex spatial structure of a scene. However, developing this capability is hindered by the cost of annotating a vast and combinatorial question space. We propose GeoX, a self-play framework that acquires spatial logic through executable programs that yield verifiable rewards, without relying on large-scale human-curated data Given a satellite or aerial image, our framework employs a single multimodal policy that proposes spatial problems as executable programs and solves them under three reasoning modes-abduction, deduction, and induction-over spatial primitives and an image understanding tool. A verifier executes each program to covert a reward signal that jointly optimizes the two roles via reinforcement learning. GeoX consistently improves its base VLMs by up to 5.5 points on average, matching or exceeding conventional baselines trained on millions of curated data. Along-side the proposed method, we release a benchmark for geospatial understanding accumulated through self-play.

### [50] [When Skills Don't Help: A Negative Result on Procedural Knowledge for Tool-Grounded Agents in Offensive Cybersecurity](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20023v2)
*Samuel Jacob Chacko,James Hugglestone,Chashi Mahiul Islam,Xiuwen Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: Agent Skills在进攻性网络安全中的负结果，直接分析agent环境反馈，有价值。

TL;DR: 在进攻性网络安全领域，Agent Skills的边际效益极小，环境反馈带宽是决定Skills是否有效的关键变量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社区缺乏对Skills何时有帮助以及何时是多余开销的清晰机制理解。

Method: 重新分析一项包含180次运行的CTF智能体控制研究，通过比较四种文档丰富度条件（对应不同Skills消融）来评估Skills的影响。

Result: 无Skills与全Skills条件之间的任务通过率差异仅8.9个百分点，统计不显著，且部分案例中Skills甚至降低性能。

Conclusion: 环境反馈带宽是关键缺失变量；当工具层提供严格、低延迟的反馈时，Skills的边际效益消失，建议复合AI系统应优先优化环境反馈而非注入Skills。

中文摘要：Agent Skills是程序化知识的结构化包，在推理时加载到LLM智能体中。据报道，它们能在不同领域将任务通过率平均提高16.2个百分点。然而，相同的基准测试显示出广泛差异，84个任务中有16个在引入Skills后出现了负的差值。社区尚未阐明Skills何时有帮助以及何时只是多余开销的清晰机制。我们重新分析了一项近期发表的、包含180次运行的控制研究，该研究涉及一个基于MCP的自主夺旗（CTF）智能体，在四种文档丰富度条件下（591、12865、17253和36001个token），并表明这些条件几乎完全对应于无技能、体验技能、精选技能和全面技能的消融实验。在进攻性网络安全领域（现有Skills基准测试未深入覆盖），Skills的边际效益崩溃。无技能和全技能条件之间的差异仅为8.9个百分点（p = 0.71，χ²；p = 0.25，Cochran-Armitage趋势检验；六对Cohen's h值中有五对低于0.2的小效应阈值）。我们认为缺失的变量是环境反馈带宽。当智能体的工具层返回严格、模式验证、低延迟的观察结果时，环境本身提供了通常需要Skills提供的程序性修正信号。因此，精选Skills的边际效益显著降低，并且在某些情况下（例如，我们的时序侧信道设置）会主动降低性能。我们提出了一个可证伪的假设，勾勒了其对复合AI系统的设计启示，并将发布再分析流程以支持复现。

Original abstract: Agent Skills, structured packages of procedural knowledge loaded into an LLM agent at inference time, are widely reported to improve task pass rates by an average of 16.2~percentage points across diverse domains. Yet the same benchmarks show wide variance, with 16 of 84 tasks suffering negative deltas when Skills are introduced. The community has not yet articulated a clean mechanism for \emph{when} Skills help and when they are merely redundant overhead. We re-analyze a recently published 180-run controlled study of an MCP-grounded autonomous Capture-the-Flag (CTF) agent under four documentation conditions of increasing richness (591, 12865, 17253, and 36001 tokens) and show that these conditions correspond almost exactly to a No-Skills, Experiential-Skills, Curated-Skills, and Comprehensive-Skills ablation. In offensive cybersecurity, a domain not deeply covered by existing Skills benchmarks, the marginal benefit of Skills collapses. The spread between the no-Skills and full-Skills conditions is only 8.9~pp ($p = 0.71$, $χ^2$; $p = 0.25$, Cochran--Armitage trend test; five of six pairwise Cohen's $h$ values fall below the $0.2$ small-effect threshold). We argue that the missing variable is \emph{environment-feedback bandwidth}. When an agent's tool layer returns strict, schema-validated, low-latency observations, the environment itself supplies the procedural correction signal that Skills are normally needed to provide. As a result, the marginal benefit of curated Skills diminishes substantially, and, in some cases (e.g., our timing side-channel setting), actively degrades performance. We articulate a falsifiable hypothesis, sketch its design implications for compound AI systems, and will release the reanalysis pipeline to support replication.

### [51] [AutoResearchClaw: Self-Reinforcing Autonomous Research with Human-AI Collaboration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20025v2)
*Jiaqi Liu,Shi Qiu,Mairui Li,Bingzhou Li,Haonian Ji,Siwei Han,Xinyu Ye,Peng Xia,Zihan Dong,Meng Chen,Congyu Zhang,Letian Zhang,Guiming Chen,Haoqin Tu,Xinyu Yang,Lu Feng,Xujiang Zhao,Haifeng Chen,Jiawei Zhou,Xiao Wang,Weitong Zhang,Hongtu Zhu,Yun Li,Jieru Mei,Hongliang Fei,Jiaheng Zhang,Linjie Li,Linjun Zhang,Yuyin Zhou,Sheng Wang,Caiming Xiong,James Zou,Zeyu Zheng,Cihang Xie,Mingyu Ding,Huaxiu Yao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent自主研究管道，包含辩论、自愈、人机协作，通用agent架构。

TL;DR: 提出AutoResearchClaw，一种多智能体自主研究流水线，通过结构化辩论、自修复执行、可验证报告、人机协作和跨运行演化，在实验基准上比AI Scientist v2提升54.7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自主研究系统将过程建模为线性流程，依赖单智能体推理，失败即停止，且不积累跨运行经验，无法模拟真实研究的迭代性。

Method: 基于五种机制：结构化多智能体辩论（假设生成与结果分析）、自修复执行器（Pivot/Refine决策循环）、可验证结果报告、七种模式的人机协作、跨运行演化。

Result: 在ARC-Bench上，AutoResearchClaw相比AI Scientist v2提升54.7%；人机协作消融表明高杠杆决策点的精准协作优于全自动或全监督。

Conclusion: AutoResearchClaw作为研究放大器，增强而非取代人类科学判断，提供开源代码。

中文摘要：自动化科学发现不仅仅是从想法生成论文。真正的研究是迭代的：假设从多个角度受到挑战，实验失败并指导下一次尝试，以及经验在循环中积累。现有的自主研究系统通常将此过程建模为线性流程：它们依赖单智能体推理，在执行失败时停止，并且不跨运行携带经验。我们提出了AutoResearchClaw，一个基于五种机制的多智能体自主研究流水线：用于假设生成和结果分析的结构化多智能体辩论，具有Pivot/Refine决策循环的自修复执行器，将失败转化为信息，可验证的结果报告防止捏造数字和幻觉引用，人机协作具有七种干预模式，从完全自主到逐步监督，以及跨运行演化将过去的错误转化为未来的保障。在ARC-Bench（一个25个主题的实验阶段基准）上，AutoResearchClaw比AI Scientist v2高出54.7%。在七种干预模式下的人机协作消融实验表明，在高杠杆决策点上的精确、有针对性的协作始终优于完全自主和详尽的逐步监督。我们将AutoResearchClaw定位为一种研究放大器，它增强而非取代人类的科学判断。代码可在https://github.com/aiming-lab/AutoResearchClaw获得。

Original abstract: Automating scientific discovery requires more than generating papers from ideas. Real research is iterative: hypotheses are challenged from multiple perspectives, experiments fail and inform the next attempt, and lessons accumulate across cycles. Existing autonomous research systems often model this process as a linear pipeline: they rely on single-agent reasoning, stop when execution fails, and do not carry experience across runs. We present AutoResearchClaw, a multi-agent autonomous research pipeline built on five mechanisms: structured multi-agent debate for hypothesis generation and result analysis, a self-healing executor with a \textsc{Pivot}/\textsc{Refine} decision loop that transforms failures into information, verifiable result reporting that prevents fabricated numbers and hallucinated citations, human-in-the-loop collaboration with seven intervention modes spanning full autonomy to step-by-step oversight, and cross-run evolution that converts past mistakes into future safeguards. On ARC-Bench, a 25-topic experiment-stage benchmark, AutoResearchClaw outperforms AI Scientist v2 by 54.7%. A human-in-the-loop ablation across seven intervention modes reveals that precise, targeted collaboration at high-leverage decision points consistently outperforms both full autonomy and exhaustive step-by-step oversight. We position AutoResearchClaw as a research amplifier that augments rather than replaces human scientific judgment. Code is available at https://github.com/aiming-lab/AutoResearchClaw.

### [52] [Probing Embodied LLMs: When Higher Observation Fidelity Hurts Problem Solving](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20072v1)
*Oussama Zenkri,Oliver Brock*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 探测具身LLM，观察保真度影响，对agent设计有启发。

TL;DR: 研究发现LLM在原始RGB输入下表现最好，在完美信息下最差，适度的动作感知噪声（40%翻转概率）能提高2.85倍成功率，原因是减少了重复动作循环，表明成功率不足以评估LLM的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在机器人任务中决策不透明，难以解释成败原因，因此需要行为性研究方法，通过控制输入信息来理解其行为模式。

Method: 使用Lockbox机械谜题，在物理机器人上比较RGB、RGB-D和真实符号观测下的LLM表现，并在模拟中随机翻转感知的行动结果来研究噪声的影响。

Result: 反直觉地，RGB输入优于完美符号观测；模拟中40%翻转概率时成功率提升2.85倍，且与重复动作减少相关。

Conclusion: 仅用成功率评估LLM可能误导，因为表现好坏可能源于感知错误与推理失败的交互，而非真正的问题解决能力。

中文摘要：大型语言模型日益被提出作为机器人系统的认知组件，然而其不透明的决策过程使得在闭环具身任务中解释成功或失败变得困难。遵循经验性AI方法论，我们通过改变代理可用的信息并测量由此产生的行为变化，行为性地研究具身LLM代理。使用Lockbox（一个具有隐藏相互依赖关系的序列机械谜题），我们在物理机器人设置中评估LLM在RGB、RGB-D和真实符号观测下的表现，并使用受控模拟来探究由此产生的行为。反直觉地，代理在原始RGB输入下表现最佳，而在完美的真实观测下表现最差。在模拟中，我们通过随机翻转感知到的行动结果来探究这一效应，发现适度的噪声能提升性能，在40%翻转概率下达到峰值，成功率比无噪声基线提高2.85倍。进一步分析将这一增益与重复动作循环的减少联系起来。这些发现表明，仅凭成功率不足以评估LLM，因为测量的性能可能反映了感知错误与推理失败之间的相互作用，而非稳健的问题解决能力。

Original abstract: Large Language Models are increasingly proposed as cognitive components for robotic systems, yet their opaque decision processes make it difficult to explain success or failure in closed-loop embodied tasks. Following an empirical AI methodology, we study embodied LLM agents behaviorally by varying the information available to the agent and measuring the resulting changes in behavior. Using the Lockbox, a sequential mechanical puzzle with hidden interdependencies, we evaluate LLMs across RGB, RGB-D, and ground-truth symbolic observations in a physical robotic setup and use controlled simulation to probe the resulting behavior. Counterintuitively, agents perform best under raw RGB input and worst under perfect ground-truth observations. In simulation, we probe this effect by randomly flipping perceived action outcomes and find that moderate noise improves performance, peaking at a 40% flip probability with a 2.85-fold success rate increase over the noise-free baseline. Further analysis links this gain to a reduction in repetitive action loops. These findings suggest that success rates alone are insufficient for evaluating LLMs, as measured performance may reflect the interaction between perceptual errors and reasoning failures rather than robust problem solving.

### [53] [Neurosymbolic Learning for Inference-Time Argumentation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20098v2)
*Gabriel Freedman,Adam Dejl,Adam Gould,Mansi,Lihu Chen,Junqi Jiang,Francesca Toni*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 神经符号推理框架，涉及LLM训练和论证，对agent推理设计有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 提出推理时论证（ITA）框架，利用形式论证语义指导LLM生成并评分论证，从而进行三元声明验证（真/假/不确定），保证预测忠实于论证结构，并在两个数据集上优于论证基线且与直接预测基线竞争。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有声明验证系统在高风险场景中缺乏处理不确定性的能力，且常依赖不忠实的后验解释。需要一种既能输出三元结果（真/假/不确定）又能提供忠实可检查论证的方法。

Method: 推理时论证（ITA）：一种可训练的神经符号框架，使用形式论证语义（1）在训练时指导LLM生成论证并分配基础分数，优化生成和评分以提升论证预测质量；（2）在推理时从生成的带分数论证计算三元预测，确保预测忠实于论证结构。

Result: 在两个三元声明验证数据集上，ITA优于基于论证的基线，并能与非论证的直接预测基线竞争，同时提供由显式可检查论证结构确定性计算的判决。

Conclusion: ITA提供了一种在声明验证中结合推理时论证的方法，实现了忠实可解释的三元预测，且性能有竞争力，有望应用于高风险场景。

中文摘要：声明验证在健康、金融等高风险的场景中是一个重要问题。当支撑声明的信息不完整或相互矛盾时，不确定的答案可能比二元真/假分类更合适。在所有情况下，对决定最终判决的考虑因素进行忠实解释至关重要。我们引入了推理时论证（ITA），这是一个可训练的神经符号框架，用于三元声明验证，其中形式论证语义（给出声明的强度）被用于（i）指导LLM训练，因为模型学习生成论证并为其分配基础分数（代表内在强度），以及（ii）从生成的、已评分的论证中计算三元（真/假/不确定）预测。因此，在训练时，论证生成和评分可以根据诱导的论证性预测的质量进行优化。此外，在推理时，最终预测在构造上忠实于决定判决的论证和分数，而不是像传统推理模型那样由可能不忠实的后验推理轨迹来证明。最后，我们展示了在两个三元声明验证数据集上，ITA改进了基于论证的基线，并且可以在提供确定性计算的、从显式可检查的论证结构中得出的判决的同时，与非论证的直接预测基线竞争。

Original abstract: Claim verification is an important problem in high-stakes settings, including health and finance. When information underpinning claims is incomplete or conflicting, uncertain answers may be more appropriate than binary true or false classifications. In all cases, faithful explanations of the considerations determining the final verdict are crucial. We introduce inference-time argumentation (ITA), a trainable neurosymbolic framework for ternary claim verification in which a formal argumentation semantics giving the strength of claims is used both (i) to guide LLM training as models learn to generate arguments and assign them base scores (representing intrinsic strengths) and (ii) to compute ternary (true/false/uncertain) predictions from generated, scored arguments. As a result, at training time, argument generation and scoring can be optimised according to the quality of the induced argumentative predictions. Moreover, at inference time, the final prediction is faithful, by construction, to the arguments and scores determining the verdict, rather than being justified by a potentially unfaithful post-hoc reasoning trace as in conventional reasoning models. We finally show that, on two datasets for ternary claim verification, ITA improves upon argumentative baselines and can perform competitively against non-argumentative direct-prediction baselines, while providing verdicts that are computed deterministically from explicit, inspectable argumentative structures.

</details>


### [54] [Using Aristotle API for AI-Assisted Theorem Proving in Lean 4: A Formalisation Case Study of the Grasshopper Problem](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20120v1)
*Gabriel Rongyang Lau*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: AI辅助定理证明agent，涉及编码和长程任务，对coding agent有参考。

TL;DR: AI辅助定理证明在奥林匹克数学中能生成大量Lean代码，但局部证明成功而全局组合步骤未解决。本文通过Grasshopper问题案例，展示了已验证的辅助引理和未解决的主定理，揭示了形式化中的核心局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 展示AI辅助形式化中局部证明与全局组合推理之间的差距，通过具体案例说明当前技术的局限性。

Method: 使用Aristotle API进行证明尝试，在Lean 4中形式化Grasshopper问题，分析生成的工件中已验证和未验证的部分。

Result: 生成了包含四个已验证辅助引理的Lean代码，但主定理因缺少全局计数步骤而留有未解决的sorrry。

Conclusion: 局部证明搜索可以成功，但全局组合书需要进一步的方法开发，AI辅助形式化在复杂数学推理中仍有显著不足。

中文摘要：AI辅助定理证明现在可以为奥林匹克级别的数学生成大量的Lean开发，但这些开发的可信度取决于哪些声明实际上被验证。本文报告了一个关于Grasshopper问题的Aristotle API证明尝试的Lean 4形式化案例研究，该问题最初作为IMO 2009问题6提出。生成的工件陈述了一个广义的Lean版本定理，包含四个经过验证的辅助引理，涉及最大性和相邻交换策略的局部组成部分，而主定理grasshopper则直接由一个未解决的sorry闭合。经过验证的组成部分确立了最终部分和等于总和、相邻交换只能影响相关的中间部分和、改变后的部分和具有预期形式，以及在允许相邻后继交换的位置上的最大性强制了一个相应的禁止集合隶属事实。Aristotle输出摘要将预期的剩余数学步骤确定为全局计数步骤，需要证明这些隶属事实至少产生n个不同的禁止值，与假设|M|<n矛盾；Lean源代码本身并未将主定理简化成一个单独编码的计数引理。本案例研究提供了一个可检查的例子，展示了AI辅助形式化的一个核心局限性，即局部证明搜索可以成功，而定理所需的全局组合簿记仍然未解决。本文贡献了一个可复现的Lean工件，并对其经过验证和未验证的证明内容进行了精确分析。

Original abstract: AI-assisted theorem proving can now generate substantial Lean developments for olympiad-level mathematics, but the evidential status of such developments depends on which declarations are actually verified. This paper reports a Lean 4 formalization case study of an Aristotle API proof attempt for the Grasshopper problem, originally posed as IMO 2009 Problem 6. The generated artifact states a generalized Lean version of the theorem, contains four verified helper lemmas for local components of a maximality and adjacent-swap exchange strategy, and leaves the main theorem grasshopper closed directly by one unresolved sorry. The verified components establish that the final partial sum equals the total sum, that an adjacent transposition can affect only the relevant intermediate partial sum, that the changed partial sum has the expected form, and that maximality at a position admitting an adjacent successor swap forces a corresponding forbidden-set membership fact. The Aristotle output summary identifies the intended remaining mathematical step as the global counting step needed to show that these membership facts produce at least n distinct forbidden values, contradicting the cardinality assumption |M| < n; the Lean source itself does not reduce the main theorem to a separately encoded counting lemma. This case study gives an inspectable example of a central limitation in AI-assisted formalization, namely that local proof search can succeed while the global combinatorial bookkeeping required for a theorem remains unresolved. The paper contributes a reproducible Lean artifact and a precise analysis of its verified and unverified proof content.

### [55] [Not Every Rubric Teaches Equally: Policy-Aware Rubric Rewards for RLVR](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20164v1)
*Utkarsh Tyagi,Xingang Guo,MohammadHossein Rezaei,Daniel George,Anas Mahmoud,Jackson Lee,Bing Liu,Yunzhong He*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 策略感知奖励权重调整，对agent自我改进和RL训练有借鉴意义。

TL;DR: 提出POW3R框架，通过策略感知的评判标准奖励权重调整，在强化学习中提升奖励信息性，加速训练并改善多项指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准静态奖励聚合将人类重要性等同于优化信号实用性，导致饱和或不可达标准干扰训练，而区分性标准权重不足。

Method: 提出POW3R框架，保留人类权重和类别平衡，利用rollout级对比动态调整标准级奖励权重，使GRPO奖励更关注当前区分策略输出的标准。

Result: 在三个基础策略、两个数据集上，POW3R在30个比较中获胜24次，平均评判标准奖励和严格完成均优于普通GRPO，训练步骤减少2.5-4倍。

Conclusion: 评判标准奖励应区分最终答案重要性和当前策略可学习信号，通过动态权重调整提升强化学习效率。

中文摘要：具有可验证奖励的强化学习在正确性可以自动检查时使后训练非常有效。然而，许多重要的模型行为需要同时满足多个定性标准。基于评判标准的奖励通过为每个提示特定标准评分并将其聚合为标量奖励来解决这一设置。然而，标准的静态聚合将标准的人类分配重要性与其当前作为优化信号的有用性混为一谈。我们表明，这一假设在评判标准强化学习中不成立：许多重要标准已经饱和或当前不可达，而区分 rollout 的标准不一定具有最大的人类权重。我们提出 POW3R，一种策略感知的评判标准奖励框架，在保留评判标准目标中的人类权重和类别平衡的同时，在训练过程中调整标准级奖励权重。POW3R 使用 rollout 级对比来强调当前区分策略输出的标准，使 GRPO 奖励更具信息性，而不改变底层评估目标。在跨多模态和纯文本设置的两个数据集上的三个基础策略中，POW3R 在 30 个基础策略/指标比较中获胜 24 次，在平均评判标准奖励和严格完成（响应满足每个所需评判标准标准的提示比例）上均优于带有评判标准奖励的普通 GRPO，并在 2.5 到 4 倍更少的训练步骤中达到相同平台。因此，评判标准奖励应区分最终答案中应重视的内容与可以教会当前策略的内容。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards has made post-training highly effective when correctness can be checked automatically. However, many important model behaviors require satisfying several qualitative criteria at once. Rubric-based rewards address this setting by grading prompt-specific criteria and aggregating them into a scalar reward. Yet standard static aggregations conflate a criterion's human-assigned importance with its current usefulness as an optimization signal. We show that this assumption breaks down in rubric RL: many important criteria are already saturated or currently unreachable, while criteria that distinguish rollouts are not necessarily those with the largest human weights. We introduce POW3R, a policy-aware rubric reward framework that preserves human weights and category balance as the rubric objective while adapting criterion-level reward weights during training. POW3R uses rollout-level contrast to emphasize criteria that currently separate the policy's outputs, making the GRPO reward more informative without changing the underlying evaluation target. Across three base policies on two datasets spanning multimodal and text-only settings, POW3R wins $24$ of $30$ base-policy/metric comparisons, improving both mean rubric reward and strict completion (the fraction of prompts whose response satisfies every required rubric criterion) over vanilla GRPO with rubric rewards, and reaches the same plateau in $2.5$--$4\times$ fewer training steps. Rubric rewards should therefore distinguish what should matter in the final answer from what can teach the current policy.

### [56] [A Methodology for Selecting and Composing Runtime Architecture Patterns for Production LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20173v1)
*Vasundra Srinivasan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出随机-确定性边界(SDB)作为生产LLM代理运行时的核心原语，并围绕它组织运行时设计，提供模式目录、选择方法论、故障诊断和可靠性分解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM代理中随机与确定性部分的边界常被忽视，导致运行时架构缺乏系统性设计。

Method: 通过定义SDB契约，划分运行时设计为协调、状态、控制三个关注点，提出六种模式，并给出五步选择方法论和故障诊断过程。

Result: 提供了应用于五个工作负载的示例和一个可运行的参考实现，识别了重放分歧故障模式。

Conclusion: 模型方差减少时，模式选择和SDB强度对长期可靠性至关重要。

中文摘要：生产型LLM代理将随机模型输出与确定性软件系统相结合，但这两者之间的边界很少被视为一等架构对象。本文将该边界命名为随机-确定性边界（SDB）：一个包含提议者、验证者、提交步骤和拒绝信号的四方契约，规定了LLM输出如何成为系统动作。我们认为SDB是生产代理运行时的基本原语。围绕这一原语，我们将代理运行时设计组织为三个关注点：协调、状态和控制。我们提出了一个包含六种运行时模式的目录，这些模式在对话型、自主型和长视野代理中以不同方式组合SDB：层次化委托、分散收集加Saga、事件驱动排序、共享状态机、监督者加门控、人在回环。对于每种模式，我们追溯其分布式系统的渊源，并指出当工作者变为随机时发生的变化。本文贡献了一个五步的运行时模式选择方法论，一个将生产故障映射到模式弱点的诊断过程，以及一个称为重放分歧的故障模式，其中基于LLM的确定性事件日志消费者在模型版本或提示变化下产生不同的下游输出。一个简化的可靠性分解将每次调用的模型方差与架构动量分开，推动了这样的主张：随着模型方差的减少，模式选择和SDB强度成为长期可靠性越来越重要的杠杆。我们将该方法应用于五个工作负载，并提供了一个为期90天的合同续签代理的可运行参考实现。

Original abstract: Production LLM agents combine stochastic model outputs with deterministic software systems, yet the boundary between the two is rarely treated as a first-class architectural object. This paper names that boundary the stochastic-deterministic boundary (SDB): a four-part contract among a proposer, verifier, commit step, and reject signal that specifies how an LLM output becomes a system action. We argue that the SDB is the load-bearing primitive of production agent runtimes.
  Around this primitive, we organize agent runtime design into three concerns: Coordination, State, and Control. We present a catalog of six runtime patterns that compose the SDB differently across conversational, autonomous, and long-horizon agents: hierarchical delegation, scatter-gather plus saga, event-driven sequencing, shared state machine, supervisor plus gate, and human in the loop. For each pattern, we trace its lineage to distributed-systems concepts and identify what changes when the worker is stochastic.
  The paper contributes a five-step methodology for selecting runtime patterns, a diagnostic procedure that maps production failures to pattern weaknesses, and a failure mode called replay divergence, in which LLM-based consumers of a deterministic event log produce different downstream outputs under model-version or prompt changes. A stylized reliability decomposition separates per-call model variance from architectural momentum, motivating the claim that as model variance decreases, pattern choice and SDB strength become increasingly important levers for long-run reliability. We apply the methodology to five workloads and provide one runnable reference implementation for a 90-day contract-renewal agent.

### [57] [OSCToM: RL-Guided Adversarial Generation for High-Order Theory of Mind](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20423v1)
*Sharmin Sultana Srishty,Kazi Mahathir Rahman,Malaika Parizat Sakkhi,Samia Shahid Prianna,Shaikhul Islam Sinat*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出高阶心智理论对抗生成方法，属于agent评测与训练增强。

TL;DR: 本文提出OSCToM，通过强化学习、扩展领域特定语言和组合代理模型生成观察者-自我冲突，在ToM基准上显著提升LLM的推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ToM基准未能充分测试递归信念和信息不对称，导致LLM在复杂社交场景中的推理能力不均。

Method: 结合强化学习、扩展的领域特定语言和组合代理模型，生成观察者-自我冲突的嵌套信念冲突数据。

Result: OSCToM-8B在FANToM上达76%准确率（对比ExploreToM的0.2%），数据合成效率提升6倍。

Conclusion: 定向训练数据可帮助小模型处理高级认知推理，OSCToM方法开源。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在许多语言任务上表现良好，但其在复杂社会场景中的心智理论（ToM）推理仍不均衡。现有基准（包括ExploreToM）并不总能测试使这些场景变得困难的递归信念和信息不对称。本文提出OSCToM（观察者-自我冲突心智理论），一种在基于LLM的ToM任务中建模嵌套信念冲突的方法。关键情景是观察者对另一智能体的看法与观察者自身的信念状态相冲突。这类情景超越了简单的视角采择，需要递归、多层推理。OSCToM结合强化学习（RL）、扩展的领域特定语言和组合代理模型来生成观察者-自我冲突。在我们的实验中，OSCToM-8B在测试系统中取得了最佳总体结果。它在FANToM上改进了已报道的ExploreToM结果，并在Hi-ToM和BigToM上保持竞争力。在信息不对称的FANToM基准上，OSCToM达到了76%的准确率，而ExploreToM报道的准确率为0.2%。数据合成过程效率也提高了6倍，表明有针对性的训练数据可以帮助较小的模型处理高级认知推理。项目代码可在https://github.com/sharminsrishty/osct获取。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) perform well on many language tasks, but their Theory of Mind (ToM) reasoning is still uneven in complex social settings. Existing benchmarks, including ExploreToM, do not always test the recursive beliefs and information asymmetries that make these settings difficult. This paper presents OSCToM (Observer-Self Conflict Theory of Mind), an approach for modeling nested belief conflicts in LLM-based ToM tasks. The key case is one in which an observer's view of another agent conflicts with the observer's own belief state. Such cases go beyond simple perspective-taking and require recursive, multi-layered reasoning. OSCToM combines reinforcement learning (RL), an extended domain-specific language, and compositional surrogate models to generate observer-self conflicts. In our experiments, OSCToM-8B gives the best overall result among the systems tested. It improves on the reported ExploreToM results on FANToM and remains competitive on Hi-ToM and BigToM. On the information-asymmetric FANToM benchmark, OSCToM reaches 76% accuracy, compared with the 0.2% reported by ExploreToM. The data-synthesis procedure is also 6x more efficient, indicating that targeted training data can help smaller models handle advanced cognitive reasoning. The project code is available at https://github.com/sharminsrishty/osct.

### [58] [AgentCo-op: Retrieval-Based Synthesis of Interoperable Multi-Agent Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20425v1)
*Shuaike Shen,Wenduo Cheng,Shike Wang,Mingqian Ma,Jian Ma*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 检索驱动的多智能体工作流合成与局部修复，直接贡献多agent协作与自动化设计。

TL;DR: AgentCo-op通过检索和局部修复组合现有技能、工具和智能体，在开放科学场景中自动生成可执行工作流，并在多项基准上取得最佳性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放科学环境中缺乏训练数据、评估指标和标准化接口，使得设计多智能体工作流极具挑战。

Method: 提出基于检索的合成框架AgentCo-op，通过类型化工件交接组装组件，并在执行失败时对相关组件进行有界自我局部修复。

Result: 在基因组学案例中成功协调专业智能体；在六个基准上取得四项最优和最佳平均分，且成本更低。

Conclusion: 检索式合成可扩展自动化工作流设计至开放世界，与搜索互补，提升可审计性和效率。

中文摘要：设计多智能体工作流在开放性的科学环境中尤其困难，因为这些任务缺乏精心策划的训练集、可靠的标量评估指标以及现有工具和智能体之间的标准化接口。我们提出了AgentCo-op，一个基于检索的合成框架，通过类型化工件交接将可复用的技能、工具和外部智能体组合成可执行的工作流，然后在执行证据表明失败时对相关组件应用有界自我指导的局部修复。在两个开放世界基因组学案例研究中，AgentCo-op无需重新设计或运行全局拓扑搜索，即可将独立开发的科学智能体和外部工具仓库组合成可审计的工作流。它协调专门用于空间转录组学和基因集解释的智能体，以支持从空间转录组数据中进行协作发现，并为单细胞多组学数据构建跨模态标记分析的并行工作流。AgentCo-op还可以将搜索到的工作流作为结构先验导入，并通过用检索到的组件接地节点和应用局部修复来改进它，这表明合成和搜索是互补的。在六个编程、数学和问答基准测试中，AgentCo-op在统一主干设置下在四个基准测试中取得了最佳结果和最佳平均分数，同时相对于多智能体基线一致降低了每任务成本。这些结果共同表明，基于检索的合成可以将自动化智能体工作流设计从基准优化的智能体图扩展到由现有智能体、工具和类型化工件构建的开放世界工作流。

Original abstract: Designing multi-agent workflows is especially difficult in open-ended scientific settings where tasks lack curated training sets, reliable scalar evaluation metrics, and standardized interfaces between existing tools and agents. We propose AgentCo-op, a retrieval-based synthesis framework that composes reusable skills, tools, and external agents into executable workflows through typed artifact handoffs, then applies bounded self-guided local repair to implicated components when execution evidence indicates failure. In two open-world genomics case studies, AgentCo-op composes independently developed scientific agents and external tool repositories into auditable workflows without redesigning them or running global topology search. It coordinates specialized agents for spatial transcriptomics and gene-set interpretation to enable collaborative discovery from spatial transcriptomics data, and builds a parallel workflow for cross-modality marker analysis on single-cell multiome data. AgentCo-op can also import a searched workflow as a structural prior and improve it by grounding nodes with retrieved components and applying local repair, showing that synthesis and search are complementary. On six coding, math, and question-answering benchmarks, AgentCo-op achieves the best result on four benchmarks and the best average score under a unified backbone setting, while consistently reducing per-task cost relative to multi-agent baselines. Together, these results suggest that retrieval-based synthesis can extend automated agentic workflow design beyond benchmark-optimized agent graphs to open-world workflows built from existing agents, tools, and typed artifacts.

</details>


### [59] [BOHM: Zero-Cost Hierarchical Attribution for Compound AI Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22866v1)
*Joss Armstrong*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出零成本层级归因方法，可应用于agent系统组件贡献分析，对理解和评估agent行为有启发。

TL;DR: BOHM直接从路由权重中提取层次归因，无需额外评估，与SHAP互补。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有归因方法如SHAP需要评估任意组件子集，不适用于集成第三方API或不透明端点的复合AI系统，而BOHM利用已存在的路由权重来解决。

Method: BOHM通过路径乘积计算叶子归因，并诱导出每层的分布作为多分辨率归因。

Result: 在多个实验上，BOHM与SHAP高度相关，但成本极低；在代理研究和人口普查数据上表现良好。

Conclusion: BOHM是一种互补原语，提供多分辨率归因，其与SHAP的不一致具有诊断价值。

中文摘要：复合AI系统通过专门组件的层次结构路由任务。归因方法主要由基于Shapley的方法（SHAP）主导，这些方法将联盟价值函数分解为每个组件的边际贡献，并要求在任意组件子集上评估系统。这一要求对于第三方API、不透明端点以及将路由集中在少数工具上的代理编排器来说无法满足，因为从已部署的编排器来看，大多数联盟是无法评估的。我们引入BOHM，它直接从这些系统已维护的路由权重中提取层次归因树：叶子归因是从根到叶子的路由权重的路径乘积；第k层归因是深度k节点上的诱导分布。该方法边际成本为零，无需访问组件内部，并同时提供每一层的多分辨率归因，这是扁平方法在任何评估预算下都无法提供的。BOHM和SHAP回答不同的问题，当部署的路由器接近最优路由时它们会收敛。在包含18个LLM的三层层次结构和880个LiveCodeBench问题上的实验中，BOHM的Kendall tau为0.928；SHAP在每种子多进行9000倍联盟评估后达到tau=0.980。在一个包含5个驱动器和7个基准的代理研究（35个单元，完全覆盖）中，驱动器将路由集中在单个工具上（最高份额中位数0.65），并且单元格级别的tau（BOHM，SHAP）可以通过驱动器的首选是否是经验上最佳的工具来预测（平均+0.22对比约+0.01）。在一个美国人口普查层次结构（475个叶子，4层）上，BOHM在每一层都恢复了真实排名（tau高达0.722）。BOHM满足效率、单调性、对称性和弱抑制性，但不满足Shapley的可加性。它最好被理解为一个互补原语：一种在存在路由状态的任何地方都可计算的多分辨率分解，其与Shapley的不一致本身具有诊断价值。

Original abstract: Compound AI systems route tasks through hierarchies of specialised components. Attribution is dominated by Shapley-based methods (SHAP), which decompose a coalition value function into per-component marginal contributions and require evaluation of the system on arbitrary component subsets. That requirement fails for third-party APIs, opaque endpoints, and agentic orchestrators that concentrate routing on a few tools, leaving most coalitions un-evaluable from the deployed orchestrator. We introduce BOHM, which extracts a hierarchical attribution tree directly from the routing weights such systems already maintain: leaf attribution is the path product of root-to-leaf routing weights; level-k attribution is the induced distribution over depth-k nodes. The method has zero marginal cost, requires no access to component internals, and provides multi-resolution attribution at every level simultaneously, which flat methods cannot offer at any evaluation budget. BOHM and SHAP answer different questions and converge when the deployed router routes near-optimally. On 18 LLMs in a 3-level hierarchy over 880 LiveCodeBench problems, BOHM yields Kendall tau=0.928; SHAP reaches tau=0.980 at 9,000x more coalition evaluations per seed. On a 5-driver, 7-benchmark agentic study (35 cells, complete coverage), drivers concentrate routing on a single tool (top-share median 0.65), and cell-level tau(BOHM,SHAP) is predicted by whether the driver's top pick is the empirically best tool (mean +0.22 vs ~+0.01). On a US Census hierarchy (475 leaves, 4 levels), BOHM recovers ground-truth rankings at every level (tau up to 0.722). BOHM satisfies efficiency, monotonicity, symmetry, and weak suppression but not Shapley's additivity. It is best understood as a complementary primitive: a multi-resolution decomposition computable wherever routing state exists, whose disagreement with Shapley is itself diagnostic.

</details>


### [60] [Open-World Evaluations for Measuring Frontier AI Capabilities](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20520v1)
*Sayash Kapoor,Peter Kirgis,Andrew Schwartz,Stephan Rabanser,J. J. Allaire,Rishi Bommasani,Harry Coppock,Magda Dubois,Gillian K Hadfield,Andrew B. Hall,Sara Hooker,Seth Lazar,Steve Newman,Dimitris Papailiopoulos,Shoshannah Tekofsky,Helen Toner,Cozmin Ududec,Arvind Narayanan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 开放世界评估方法，用于衡量AI agent真实任务能力，对agent评测有直接启发。

TL;DR: 本文提出开放世界评估作为基准评估的补充，并通过一个AI代理开发iOS应用的案例展示了其提供能力早期预警的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基准评估可能高估或低估AI能力，因为它偏向简单、可自动化任务，需要更真实的评估来反映部署能力。

Method: 综述近期开放世界评估，介绍CRUX项目，并实施一个AI代理开发并发布iOS应用的实验作为实例。

Result: AI代理仅需一次可避免的人工干预即完成iOS应用开发与发布，表明开放世界评估能早期预警可能很快普及的能力。

Conclusion: 建议采用开放世界评估作为基准评估的补充，并给出了设计和报告此类评估的推荐做法。

中文摘要：基于基准的评估对于跟踪前沿人工智能进展仍然重要。但它可能既高估又低估已部署的能力，因为它偏向那些可以精确指定、自动评分、易于优化、且以低预算和短时间跨度运行的任务。我们提倡一种互补的评估类别，称为开放世界评估：长期、杂乱、真实世界的任务，通过小样本定性分析而非基准规模的自动化来评估。在本文中，我们综述了最近的开放世界评估，识别了它们的优势和局限性，并介绍了CRUX（Collaborative Research for Updating AI eXpectations），一个定期进行此类评估的项目。作为第一个实例，我们让一个AI代理开发并发布一个简单的iOS应用到苹果应用商店。代理仅通过一次可避免的人工干预就完成了任务，这表明开放世界评估可以为可能很快变得普遍的能力提供早期预警。最后，我们提出了设计和报告开放世界评估的建议。

Original abstract: Benchmark-based evaluation remains important for tracking frontier AI progress. But it can both overstate and understate deployed capability because it privileges tasks that can be precisely specified, automatically graded, easy to optimize for, and run with low budgets and short time horizons. We advocate for a complementary class of evaluations, which we term open-world evaluations: long-horizon, messy, real-world tasks assessed through small-sample qualitative analysis rather than benchmark-scale automation. In this paper we survey recent open-world evaluations, identify their strengths and limitations, and introduce CRUX (Collaborative Research for Updating AI eXpectations), a project for conducting such evaluations regularly. As a first instance, we task an AI agent with developing and publishing a simple iOS application to the Apple App Store. The agent completed the task with only a single avoidable manual intervention, suggesting that open-world evaluations can provide early warning of capabilities that may soon become widespread. We conclude with recommendations for designing and reporting open-world evals.

</details>


### [61] [AgentAtlas: Beyond Outcome Leaderboards for LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20530v2)
*Parsa Mazaheri,Kasra Mazaheri*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: AgentAtlas是一个诊断框架，通过控制决策分类法和轨迹失败词汇表，将智能体评估从仅关注结果成功扩展到行为质量分析，揭示了基准覆盖和评估中的测量风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体评估只关注最终任务成功，忽略了控制决策和轨迹质量，导致诊断不足和隐藏失败。

Method: 提出六状态控制决策分类法、轨迹失败词汇表、基准覆盖审计和合成数据集上的协议研究，对比分类法感知与盲提示格式。

Result: 合成演示显示，移除显式标签菜单会改变映射标签一致性，且轴选择改变排名，说明测量风险。

Conclusion: AgentAtlas帮助基准设计者和评估者覆盖和诊断行为，弥补结果导向评估的不足。

中文摘要：大型语言模型智能体现在可以操作代码库、浏览器、操作系统、日历、文件和工具生态系统，但它们的评估往往将行为简化为最终任务成功。AgentAtlas将智能体评估重新构建为一个诊断词汇表和审计协议，用于将结果成功与控制决策质量和轨迹质量分开。本文贡献了：(i) 一个六状态控制决策分类法（行动/询问/拒绝/停止/确认/恢复）；(ii) 一个包含主要错误源和下游影响的轨迹失败词汇表；(iii) 一个针对十五个智能体基准的0/1/2基准覆盖审计；(iv) 一个在合成1,342项数据集上进行的说明性协议研究，使用八个模型在分类法感知和分类法盲的提示格式下进行评估。该合成演示不是公开基准发布，不应被视为确定的模型比较。相反，它说明了两个测量风险：当显式标签菜单被移除时，映射标签一致性可能发生显著变化，并且轴的选择可能改变明显的排名。AgentAtlas旨在帮助基准设计者阐明它们覆盖的行为，并帮助评估者诊断仅结果导向的排行榜所隐藏的失败。

Original abstract: Large language model agents now act on codebases, browsers, operating systems, calendars, files, and tool ecosystems, but their evaluations often collapse behavior into final task success. AgentAtlas reframes agent evaluation as a diagnostic vocabulary and audit protocol for separating outcome success from control-decision quality and trajectory quality. The paper contributes: (i) a six-state control-decision taxonomy (Act / Ask / Refuse / Stop / Confirm / Recover); (ii) a trajectory-failure vocabulary with primary error source and downstream impact; (iii) a 0/1/2 benchmark-coverage audit over fifteen agent benchmarks; and (iv) an illustrative protocol study on a synthetic 1,342-item set evaluated with eight models under taxonomy-aware and taxonomy-blind prompt formats. The synthetic demonstration is not a public benchmark release and should not be read as a definitive model comparison. Instead, it illustrates two measurement risks: mapped label agreement can change substantially when the explicit label menu is removed, and axis choice can change apparent rankings. AgentAtlas is intended to help benchmark designers state what behavior they cover, and to help evaluators diagnose failures that outcome-only leaderboards hide.

</details>

### [62] [PrefBench: Evaluating Zero-Shot LLM Agents in Hidden-Preference Personalized Pricing Negotiations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22855v1)
*Yingjie Lei*

Main category: cs.GT

Selection reason: 隐藏偏好议价agent评测，可启发agent隐偏好建模

TL;DR: 提出了PrefBench基准，发现LLM在个性化定价谈判中虽能高成交率但利润低下，表明结构合规与盈利决策可分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在个性化定价谈判中缺乏基准，且成功交互不保证盈利，亟需一个隐藏偏好下的可控评估环境。

Method: 构建PrefBench模拟器，每回合配对模拟买方与固定套餐，卖方通过LLM状态摘要协议返回JSON动作，在隐藏信息边界下评估零样本LLM卖方与启发式对比。

Result: LLM成交率超过0.99，但最佳平均利润仅略高于随机基线，远低于简单让步启发式。

Conclusion: 结构化的行动合规与寻求协议行为可与弱利润敏感议价共存，PrefBench为评估隐藏偏好下的定价智能体提供了受控基准。

中文摘要：个性化定价谈判对于LLM智能体来说是一个具有挑战性的试验场，因为成功的交互并不能保证盈利的决策。当买方的支付意愿和议价特征仍然隐藏时，卖方可能产生有效的行动并完成许多交易，但定价仍然不佳。本文提出了PrefBench，一个基于模拟器的基准测试，用于隐藏偏好的个性化定价谈判。每个回合将一个模拟买方与一个固定的车辆定制套餐配对；卖方观察公共人物描述符、套餐信息和谈判历史，而潜在的买方变量控制估值、耐心、还价行为和放弃决策。PrefBench通过一个面向LLM的状态摘要协议来评估这一设置，该协议在固定的隐藏信息边界下约束智能体返回严格的JSON动作。我们评估了零样本LLM卖方在7500个回合中与启发式参考的对比。测试的LLM可靠地遵循协议，实现了超过0.99的成交率，但其卖方利润结果仍然较弱：最佳LLM平均利润仅略高于随机基线，远低于同一回合流下的简单让步启发式。这些结果表明，结构化的行动合规性和寻求协议的行为可以与弱的利润敏感议价共存。PrefBench为在隐藏买方偏好下评估定价智能体行为提供了一个受控基准。

Original abstract: Personalized pricing negotiations are a challenging testbed for LLM agents because successful interaction does not guarantee profitable decision making. A seller may produce valid actions and close many deals while still pricing poorly when buyer willingness to pay and bargaining traits remain hidden. This paper presents PrefBench, a simulator-based benchmark for hidden-preference personalized pricing negotiations. Each episode pairs a simulated buyer with a fixed vehicle-customization bundle; the seller observes public persona descriptors, bundle information, and negotiation history, while latent buyer variables govern valuation, patience, counter-offer behavior, and walkaway decisions. PrefBench evaluates this setting through an LLM-facing state-summary protocol that constrains agents to return strict JSON actions under a fixed hidden-information boundary. We evaluate zero-shot LLM sellers against heuristic references over 7,500 episodes. The tested LLMs follow the protocol reliably and achieve deal rates above 0.99, but their seller-profit outcomes remain weak: the best LLM average profit is only slightly above the random baseline and far below a simple concession heuristic under the same episode stream. These results show that structured action compliance and agreement-seeking behavior can coexist with weak profit-sensitive bargaining. PrefBench provides a controlled benchmark for evaluating pricing-agent behavior under hidden buyer preferences.

</details>
