# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [94] [Smaller Abstract State Spaces Enable Cross-Scale Generalization in Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20272v1)
*Nasehatul Mustakim,Lucas Lehnert*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: RL抽象状态空间减小可提升OOD泛化，对agent抽象规划有启发

TL;DR: 本文提出了第一个理论模型，证明通过抽象状态空间压缩可以实现强化学习中的分布外泛化，并推导了性能界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管人类擅长抽象概念泛化，但强化学习系统在分布外泛化上仍困难，缺乏理论指导。

Method: 将状态抽象框架扩展到POMDP，定义后继加权模型简化，推导OOD泛化性能界限，并分解性能损失为近似和估计误差。

Result: 得出了OOD泛化性能的界限，表明减小抽象状态空间大小能提高测试性能和泛化能力，且约束智能体于小有限抽象状态集是必要的。

Conclusion: 鼓励进一步研究跨复杂度任务扩展的RL架构，强调抽象状态空间压缩的关键作用。

中文摘要：虽然人类很容易将抽象概念泛化到更复杂或更大的任务，但构建具有这种能力的强化学习（RL）系统仍然难以实现。在这里，我们提出了第一个关于如何在RL智能体中实现这种分布外（OOD）泛化的理论模型。我们的方法考虑部分可观察马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP），并假设智能体使用抽象函数来确定哪些经验可以视为等价，哪些必须区分。首先，我们将现有的状态抽象框架和证明技术扩展到POMDP。然后，我们定义了一种后继加权模型简化，这是一种模型简化变体，能够比先前定义允许的更小的抽象空间进行压缩。我们推导了智能体OOD测试性能的界限，从而定义了OOD泛化可实现的条件。该界限将智能体的性能损失分解为近似误差和估计误差，揭示了减小智能体抽象状态空间大小如何提高测试性能和OOD泛化。我们的分析表明，约束智能体在一个小的、有限的抽象状态集上操作是实现向更复杂任务泛化的必要条件。我们的结果鼓励进一步研究学习跨不同复杂度任务扩展的RL架构。

Original abstract: While humans readily generalize abstract concepts to more complex or larger tasks, building Reinforcement Learning (RL) systems with this ability remains elusive. Here, we present the first theoretical model of how such Out-of-Distribution (OOD) generalization can be achieved in RL agents. Our approach considers Partially Observable Markov Decision Processes (POMDPs) and assumes that an intelligent agent uses an abstraction function to determine which experiences can be treated as equivalent and which must be distinguished. First, we extend the existing state abstraction framework and proof techniques to POMDPs. Then, we define a successor-weighted model reduction, a model reduction variant that enables compression into smaller abstract spaces than prior definitions allow. We derive a bound on the agent's OOD test performance, thereby defining the conditions under which OOD generalization is achievable. This bound decomposes an agent's performance loss into approximation and estimation errors, revealing how reducing an agent's abstract state space size improves test performance and OOD generalization. Our analysis suggests that constraining an agent to operate over a small, finite set of abstract states is necessary for achieving generalization to more complex tasks. Our results motivate further research into learning RL architectures that scale across tasks of varying complexity levels.

</details>


### [95] [EviTrack: Selection over Sampling for Delayed Disambiguation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19283v1)
*Omer Haq*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 轨迹选择延迟消歧，类似agent多假设跟踪，有规划潜力

TL;DR: 提出了EviTrack，一种通过轨迹级假设选择应对延迟消歧的测试时推理框架，在合成基准上优于采样基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准边际推理方法在延迟消歧中要么过早坍缩不确定性，要么无法恢复，需要更好的延迟承诺策略。

Method: EviTrack在潜在轨迹上维护一组竞争假设，通过证据和似然比选择推迟决策，借鉴多假设跟踪和检测前跟踪思想。

Result: 在合成的延迟消歧基准上，EviTrack在匹配推理预算下显著优于采样基线，实现更快的消歧后恢复。

Conclusion: 延迟消歧场景中，适度的轨迹级选择比增加采样覆盖更有效，选择优于采样是可靠序列推理的关键原则。

中文摘要：序列预测在延迟消歧的场景中具有挑战性，在这种场景中，早期观测是模糊的，多个潜在解释在足够证据积累之前仍然合理。基于边际推理的标准方法在这种设置下表现不佳，要么过早地消除不确定性，要么在信息性证据到达后无法恢复。我们引入了EviTrack，一种在测试时进行推理的框架，它在潜在轨迹上而非边际状态上操作。EviTrack维护一组竞争的轨迹假设，并应用基于证据和似然比的选择来推迟承诺，直到数据支持为止，其灵感来自多假设跟踪和检测前跟踪中的假设管理。为了评估这种设置，我们构建了一个受控的合成基准，具有已知的潜在真实状态，明确表现出延迟消歧。在匹配的推理预算下，EviTrack显著优于基于采样的基线，实现了更快的消歧后恢复。这些结果表明，在延迟消歧场景中，适度的轨迹级选择比增加采样覆盖更有效，强调了选择优于采样作为可靠序列推理的关键原则。

Original abstract: Sequential prediction is challenging in regimes of delayed disambiguation, where early observations are ambiguous and multiple latent explanations remain plausible until sufficient evidence accumulates. Standard approaches based on marginal inference struggle in this setting, either collapsing uncertainty prematurely or failing to recover once informative evidence arrives.
  We introduce EviTrack, a test-time inference framework that operates over latent trajectories rather than marginal states. EviTrack maintains a set of competing trajectory hypotheses and applies evidence- and likelihood-ratio-based selection to delay commitment until supported by data, drawing inspiration from hypothesis management in multiple hypothesis tracking and track-before-detect.
  To evaluate this setting, we construct a controlled synthetic benchmark with known latent ground truth that explicitly exhibits delayed disambiguation. At matched inference budget, EviTrack substantially outperforms sampling-based baselines, achieving faster post-disambiguation recovery.
  These results show that, in delayed disambiguation regimes, moderate trajectory-level selection is more effective than increasing sampling coverage, highlighting selection over sampling as a key principle for reliable sequential inference.

### [96] [The Evaluation Game: Beyond Static LLM Benchmarking](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19377v1)
*Paul Wang,Jade Garcia-Bourrée,Anne-Marie Kermarrec,Vincent Corruble*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 博弈论框架评估LLM鲁棒性，对agent评估有启发。

TL;DR: 本文提出一个博弈论框架，使用群作用形式化数据增强，揭示了微调防御的局部泛化特性，并重新定义了对抗性评估基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 越狱攻击不断出现，微调作为防御但理论基础不足，需要理论框架理解鲁棒性微调的本质。

Method: 构建评估者与训练者的双人博弈模型，引入群作用表示数据增强，分析圆上的循环平移群实例，进行经验验证。

Result: 发现临界阈值下评估者保持恒定漏报率；微调仅诱导局部泛化，拒绝率与距离高度相关；基准测试应视为轨道而非静态集。

Conclusion: 框架表明审计需考虑训练者适应，仅靠静态基准无法区分真正修复和记忆补丁。

中文摘要：随着对抗性设计的输入（即绕过安全约束的越狱攻击）在大型语言模型中不断被发现，从业者越来越依赖微调作为防御策略。然而，这种鲁棒性微调背后的理论基础仍未得到充分探索。我们引入了一个博弈论框架，将评估者（对模型进行越狱审计）与训练者之间的互动形式化为一个双人博弈。我们方法的一个关键特征是使用群作用（一种捕捉对称性和变换的数学结构）来形式化数据增强。最简单的非平凡实例是具有循环平移群的圆，我们根据训练者的泛化范围展示了各种不同的状态。低于某个临界阈值时，评估者在线性多轮中保持恒定的漏报率，而其他设置可能产生非常不同的行为。我们进一步提供了支持模型局部依赖性的经验证据：对于我们测试的三个模型系列（Llama、Qwen和Mistral），我们有显著证据表明，对抗性提示的微调仅能诱导局部泛化，测试示例的拒绝率与到微调提示的距离高度相关。我们的框架重构了对抗性评估的核心对象：基准测试不是一组静态的提示，而是评估者群作用下的轨道，而忽略训练者侧适应的审计协议无法区分真正的修复和记忆补丁。

Original abstract: As jailbreaks, adversarially crafted inputs that bypass safety constraints, continue to be discovered in Large Language Models, practitioners increasingly rely on fine-tuning as a defensive strategy. Yet the theoretical foundations underlying this robustness fine-tuning remain underexplored. We introduce a game-theoretic framework in which the interaction between an evaluator (auditing the model for jailbreaks) and a trainer is formalized as a two-player game.
  A key feature of our approach is the use of group actions, a mathematical structure that captures symmetries and transformations, to formally represent data augmentation. The simplest non-trivial instance is the circle with cyclic translation groups, where we exhibit various regimes depending on the trainer's generalization range. Below a critical threshold, the evaluator maintains a constant miss ratio for linearly many rounds, whereas other settings can yield very different behaviors. We further provide empirical evidence supporting locality-dependence of the model: for the three model families we tested (Llama, Qwen and Mistral), we have significant evidence that fine-tuning on adversarial prompts induces only local generalization, with refusal rates on test examples highly correlated with the distance to the fine-tuning prompts. Our framework recasts the central object of adversarial evaluation: a benchmark is not a static set of prompts but an orbit under the evaluator's group action, and audit protocols that ignore trainer-side adaptation cannot distinguish a genuine fix from a memorized patch.

### [97] [Introspective X Training: Feedback Conditioning Improves Scaling Across all LLM Training Stages](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20285v1)
*Brandon Cui,Ximing Lu,Jaehun Jung,Syeda Nahida Akter,Hyunwoo Kim,Yuxiao Qu,David Acuna,Shrimai Prabhumoye,Yejin Choi,Prithviraj Ammanabrolu*

Selection reason: 反馈条件化训练方法，提升代码和数学性能，对agent训练机制有启发。

TL;DR: 提出内省训练（IXT），利用后训练阶段的反馈指导预训练，通过思维奖励模型和前缀条件化实现质量感知训练，在7.5-12B模型上最高提升2.8倍计算效率，并在数学和代码领域达到超越传统训练的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM训练管线中，后期阶段（如后训练）的动态可用于指导前期阶段（如预训练），从而更有效地扩展训练过程。

Method: IXT方法受离线奖励条件强化学习启发，使用思维奖励模型生成自然语言批评反馈来标注数据，并通过前缀条件化使模型从训练早期就能区分不同质量的token。

Result: 在7.5-12B transformer模型上训练至18万亿token，IXT实现了最高2.8倍的计算效率提升，并在数学和代码领域达到了传统训练无法企及的性能。

Conclusion: IXT通过利用后训练阶段的反馈来指导早期训练，能显著弯曲缩放曲线，提升计算效率并突破性能上限，尤其适用于数学和代码等复杂领域。

中文摘要：我们探讨了如何更高效地扩展当前LLM训练管线中众多且不断增长的阶段。我们的指导直觉源于这样一个事实：管线后期阶段（例如后训练）的动态可用于指导前期阶段（例如预训练）。为此，我们提出了内省训练（IXT），其灵感来自离线奖励条件强化学习，并适用于训练的任何阶段。IXT使用思维奖励模型用基于自然语言批评的反馈来标注数据，从而从管线最早阶段实现质量感知训练。然后，通过用生成的反馈对数据进行前缀条件化来训练模型——确保并非所有token从训练早期就受到同等对待。在从头训练直到看到18万亿token的7.5-12B基于Transformer的密集LLM上的全面实验表明，我们的方法：通常弯曲缩放曲线，导致高达2.8倍的计算效率提升；并在数学和代码等领域达到了其他训练的模型无法达到的性能水平。

Original abstract: We tackle the question of how to scale more efficiently across the many, ever-growing stages of current LLM training pipelines. Our guiding intuition stems from the fact that the dynamics of later stages of the pipeline, e.g. post-training, can be used to inform earlier stages such as pre-training. To this end, we propose Introspective Training (or IXT), inspired by offline reward-conditioned reinforcement learning and applicable to any stage of training. IXT uses a thinking reward model to annotate data with natural language critique based feedback, enabling quality aware training from the earliest stages of the pipeline. Models are then trained by prefix-conditioning the data with the generated feedback -- ensuring that not all tokens are treated equally starting much earlier in training than usual. Comprehensive experiments on 7.5-12B transformer-based dense LLMs trained from scratch all the way up to 18 Trillion tokens seen show that our method: bends scaling curves resulting in up to 2.8x more compute efficiency generally; and reaches performance levels unachievable for models trained otherwise in domains such as math and code.

### [98] [When to Stop Reusing: Dynamic Gradient Gating for Sample-Efficient RLVR](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19425v1)
*Yuchun Miao,Sen Zhang,Yuqi Zhang,Yaorui Shi,Qi Gu,Xunliang Cai,Lefei Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: RLVR样本效率改进，动态梯度门控方法可应用于agent强化学习。

TL;DR: 通过识别DWD现象，利用lm_head梯度范数作为实时信号，提出DGG方法，在RLVR中实现高达2.93倍样本效率和2.14倍速度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RLVR中重复使用rollout批次进行多次梯度更新会加剧策略偏移导致性能退化，而早期检测退化并停止复用是开放问题。

Method: 识别DWD现象（性能退化与lm_head权重剧增同步），理论上证明lm_head梯度范数下界政策散度，提出DGG实时监控并拦截有害梯度。

Result: DGG在数学、ALFWorld、WebShop和搜索增强QA任务上匹配或超过单次使用基线，样本效率最高2.93倍，墙钟加速最高2.14倍。

Conclusion: DWD现象和lm_head梯度范数可作为RLVR中监测策略偏移的有效信号，DGG方法显著提升样本效率与速度。

中文摘要：可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）已成为大型语言模型（LLMs）高级推理的主流范式，但生成rollout样本成本高昂，使得样本效率成为关键瓶颈。一种自然的补救措施是重复使用每个rollout批次进行多次梯度更新，这是经典RL中的标准做法。然而，在RLVR中，这会加剧策略偏移，导致严重的性能退化。在早期阶段检测到退化的开始并停止复用仍是一个开放且具有挑战性的问题。我们通过识别“不成比例权重发散（DWD）”现象来填补这一空白：性能退化与lm_head权重变化的急剧飙升同步发生，而中间层保持稳定。实验上，我们验证了DWD在各种LLMs和任务中一致出现。理论上，我们证明了（i）有害梯度集中在lm_head，而中间层在结构上被衰减，以及（ii）lm_head梯度范数下界于策略散度。这些结果确立了lm_head梯度范数作为灾难性策略偏移的一个原则性、实时信号。基于这一见解，我们提出了动态梯度门控（DGG），这是一种轻量级的干预措施，它实时监视lm_head梯度范数，并在有害梯度破坏优化器之前将其拦截。DGG一致达到或超过标准的单次使用基线，在数学、ALFWorld、WebShop和搜索增强QA任务上实现了高达2.93倍的样本效率和2.14倍的墙钟加速。

Original abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has become the dominant paradigm for advanced reasoning in Large Language Models (LLMs), but rollout samples are expensive to obtain, making sample efficiency a critical bottleneck. A natural remedy is to reuse each rollout batch for multiple gradient updates, a standard practice in classical RL. Yet in RLVR, this amplifies policy shift, leading to severe performance degradation. Detecting the onset of degradation early enough to stop reuse remains an open and challenging problem. We close this gap by identifying the \textit{Disproportionate Weight Divergence (DWD)} phenomenon: performance degradation is synchronized with a sharp surge in the \texttt{lm\_head} weight change, while intermediate layers remain stable. Empirically, we verify that DWD emerges consistently across diverse LLMs and tasks. Theoretically, we prove that (i) harmful gradients concentrate at the \texttt{lm\_head} while intermediate layers are structurally attenuated, and (ii) the \texttt{lm\_head} gradient norm lower-bounds the policy divergence. These results establish the \texttt{lm\_head} gradient norm as a principled, real-time signal of catastrophic policy shift. Guided by this insight, we propose \textit{Dynamic Gradient Gating (DGG)}, a lightweight intervention that monitors the \texttt{lm\_head} gradient norm in real time and intercepts harmful gradients before they corrupt the optimizer. DGG consistently matches or exceeds the standard single-use baseline, achieving up to $2.93\times$ sample efficiency and $2.14\times$ wall-clock speedup across math, ALFWorld, WebShop, and search-augmented QA tasks.

### [99] [Sampling-Based Safe Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19469v1)

中文摘要：安全探索仍然是强化学习中的一个基本挑战，限制了强化学习智能体在现实世界中的部署。我们提出了基于采样的安全强化学习（SBSRL），这是一种基于模型的强化学习算法，通过在一组有限的动力学样本上联合施加约束，在整个学习过程中保持安全性。这种公式近似于不确定动力学上的难处理最坏情况优化，并在连续域中实现了实际的安全保证。我们进一步引入了一种基于约束认知不确定性的探索策略，消除了对显式探索奖励的需求。在正则条件下，我们推导了整个学习过程中安全性的高概率保证，以及恢复近最优策略的有限时间样本复杂度界。实验上，SBSRL在仿真和真实机器人硬件上都实现了安全高效的探索，并且很容易扩展到实用的深度集成实现，能够扩展到高维连续控制问题。

Original abstract: Safe exploration remains a fundamental challenge in reinforcement learning (RL), limiting the deployment of RL agents in the real world. We propose Sampling-Based Safe Reinforcement Learning (SBSRL), a model-based RL algorithm that maintains safety throughout the learning process by enforcing constraints jointly across a finite set of dynamics samples. This formulation approximates an intractable worst-case optimization over uncertain dynamics and enables practical safety guarantees in continuous domains. We further introduce an exploration strategy based on constraining epistemic uncertainty, eliminating the need for explicit exploration bonuses. Under regularity conditions, we derive high-probability guarantees of safety throughout learning and a finite-time sample complexity bound for recovering a near-optimal policy. Empirically, SBSRL achieves safe and efficient exploration both in simulation and in real robotic hardware, and readily extends to practical deep-ensemble implementations that scale to high-dimensional continuous control problems.

Result: MnLP在各种问题规模和分布上提升泛化能力，优于现有方法，且无额外推理开销。

Conclusion: MnLP有效增强神经策略的长期上下文理解，可无缝集成到多种架构中。

中文摘要：神经策略因减少对手工启发式方法的依赖，在解决车辆路径问题方面显示出潜力。然而，当前的训练范式存在一个根本性限制：它们主要关注解构建中的下一个节点预测，导致短视决策，削弱了长期规划能力。为此，我们引入了多节点前瞻预测（MnLP），这是一种新颖的训练策略，它将监督学习范式扩展到同时预测多个未来节点。我们引入了仅在训练期间运行的因果性和可丢弃的MnLP模块，使模型能够预见多步决策，同时保持推理时的效率。通过将多深度辅助监督纳入损失函数，MnLP赋予了神经策略长期上下文理解能力。实验表明，MnLP优于现有的训练方法，提升了神经策略在各种问题规模、分布和真实世界基准上的泛化能力。此外，MnLP可以无缝集成到多种神经架构中，且不会引入额外的推理开销。

Original abstract: Neural policies have shown promise in solving vehicle routing problems due to their reduced reliance on handcrafted heuristics. However, current training paradigms suffer from a fundamental limitation: they primarily focus on next-node prediction for solution construction, resulting in myopic decision-making that undermines long-horizon planning capacity. To this end, we introduce Multi-node Lookahead Prediction (MnLP), a novel training strategy that extends the supervised learning paradigm to predict multiple future nodes simultaneously. We incorporate causal and discardable MnLP modules that operate exclusively during training, facilitating models to anticipate multi-step decisions while preserving inference-time efficiency. By incorporating multi-depth auxiliary supervision into the loss function, MnLP equips neural policies with the ability of long-range contextual understanding. Experimentally, MnLP outperforms existing training methods, improving the generalization capability of neural policies across various problem sizes, distributions, and real-world benchmarks. Moreover, MnLP can be seamlessly integrated into diverse neural architectures without introducing additional inference overhead.

</details>


### [101] [CAFD: Concept-Aware DNN Fault Detection using VLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24008v1)
*Amin Abbasishahkoo,Mahboubeh Dadkhah,Lionel Briand*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出概念感知故障检测（CAFD），通过整合模型、距离和概念特征实现高效准确的DNN故障检测，平均FDR提高18.3%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有混合故障检测方法虽然性能好但计算开销大，限制了实际应用；需要一种既有效又高效的方法。

Method: 提出CAFD，利用模型信号、距离特征和基于视觉语言模型的新颖概念特征（CFR）进行训练，融合多种信息源。

Result: 在三个DNN模型和数据集上，CAFD在FDR上平均比五个基线提高18.3%，并优于所有对比方法。

Conclusion: CAFD是一种高效且有效的DNN故障检测方法，CFR作为特征能显著提升检测性能。

中文摘要：深度神经网络（DNN）的故障检测近年来受到越来越多的关注。虽然更先进的混合方法已被提出以结合多种信息源并优于早期技术，但它们通常会带来大量的计算开销，限制了在现实环境中的可扩展性和实用性。在本文中，我们引入了概念感知故障检测（CAFD），一种基于学习的方法，通过有效整合多种信息源同时保持实际效率，实现了卓越的故障检测性能。具体来说，CAFD使用一组精心选择的信息特征进行训练，包括基于DNN输出的模型信号、基于距离的特征以及一种新颖的基于概念的特征，称为概念故障比（CFR）。CFR利用视觉语言模型（VLM）从图像中提取文本概念，并量化其存在与DNN故障相关的可能性。通过融入这一特征，CAFD受益于互补的语义信息，从而实现更有效的故障检测。我们的结果表明，CFR是DNN故障检测的有效指标。我们对CAFD进行了广泛的经验评估，将其与五种最先进的基线方法在三个主题DNN模型和数据集（包括ImageNet）上进行比较。在广泛的受约束选择预算内，CAFD在故障检测率（FDR）上始终优于所有基线，在所有研究主题和预算规模上平均FDR提高了18.3%。

Original abstract: Fault detection for Deep Neural Networks (DNNs) has received increasing attention in recent years. While more advanced hybrid approaches have been proposed to combine multiple sources of information and outperform earlier techniques, they often incur substantial computational overhead, limiting scalability and practicality in real-world settings. In this paper, we introduce Concept-Aware Fault Detection (CAFD), a learning-based approach that achieves superior fault detection performance by effectively integrating multiple information sources while maintaining practical efficiency. Specifically, CAFD is trained using a carefully selected set of informative features, including model-based signals derived from the DNN's outputs, distance-based features, and a novel concept-based feature, called Concept Failure Ratio (CFR). CFR leverages Vision-Language Models (VLMs) to extract textual concepts from images and quantify the likelihood that their presence is associated with DNN failures. By incorporating this feature, CAFD benefits from complementary semantic information, enabling more effective fault detection. Our results demonstrate that CFR serves as an effective indicator for DNN fault detection. We conduct an extensive empirical evaluation of CAFD, comparing it against five state-of-the-art baselines across three subject DNN models and datasets, including ImageNet. Across a wide range of constrained selection budgets, CAFD consistently outperforms all baselines in Fault Detection Rate (FDR), achieving average FDR improvements of 18.3% across all investigated subjects and budget sizes.

</details>


### [102] [Training Language Agents to Learn from Experience](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20477v1)
*Yuval Shalev,Zifeng Ding,Mateja Jamnik*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出语言agent从经验中学习跨任务改进的框架，包含RL训练和反射生成，直接相关agent通用方法。

TL;DR: 本文提出上下文训练（ICT）任务和基于强化学习的训练流程，使语言代理能够从经验中学习跨任务自我改进，并在多个环境中验证了效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前反思方法仅限于单任务自我修正，无法跨任务复用经验，需要探索如何从经验中提炼可重用的教训以提升未来任务性能。

Method: 提出了ICT任务框架，其中反射器模型根据演员模型轨迹生成系统提示以改进未来任务表现；然后利用强化学习训练反射器，无需人工示例。

Result: 在ALFWorld和MiniHack上，训练的反射器在多数保留任务族上优于未训练基线，并展现出跨环境泛化能力。

Conclusion: 证明了从经验中学习的能力本身可被学习，并提供了MetaGym库以促进后续研究。

中文摘要：语言代理可以在交互环境中从经验中适应，但当前基于反思的方法只能在单个任务实例内进行自我修正。这种经验能否被提炼为可重用的经验教训，从而提高未来未见任务的性能，仍不清楚。我们通过引入上下文训练（ICT）任务来解决这个问题，这是一个用于评估语言代理跨任务自我改进的框架。在ICT中，反射器模型观察由演员模型收集的轨迹，并生成旨在改善演员在未来未见任务上表现的系统提示。然后，我们提出了一种基于强化学习的训练流程，直接从经验中学习这种反思，无需人工提供的示例。在ALFWorld和MiniHack上，我们训练的反射器在大多数保留任务族上优于未训练的基线，表明从经验中学习的能力本身是可以学习的。在某些情况下，我们观察到反射器在其训练的基准之外，能泛化到截然不同的环境。最后，我们介绍了MetaGym，一个用于构建元环境的通用Python库，为自改进语言代理的未来研究提供支持。

Original abstract: Language agents can adapt from experience in interactive environments, but current reflection-based methods can only self-correct within a single task instance. Whether such experience can be distilled into reusable lessons that improve performance on future unseen tasks remains unclear. We address this problem by introducing the In-context Training (ICT) task, a framework for evaluating cross-task self-improvement in language agents. In ICT, a reflector model observes trajectories collected by an actor model and generates system prompts intended to improve the actor's performance on future unseen tasks. We then propose an RL-based training pipeline for learning such reflections directly from experience, without human-provided examples. Across ALFWorld and MiniHack, our trained reflectors outperform an untrained baseline on most held-out task families, showing that the ability to learn from experience can itself be learned. In some cases, we observe generalisation beyond the benchmark on which the reflector was trained, to substantially different environments. Finally, we introduce MetaGym, a generic Python library for constructing meta-environments, enabling future research on self-improving language agents.

</details>

### [103] [ContextFlow: Hierarchical Task-State Alignment for Long-Horizon Embodied Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19314v1)
*Shuhan Guo,Kun Zhang,Haifei Liu,Xingyu Gao,Yongqi Zhang,Yaqing Wang,Quanming Yao*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 长程具身agent的任务状态对齐框架，可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: ContextFlow通过显式契约和证据包检测并修复任务状态不对齐，提升长时程具身任务的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着执行器变强，主要瓶颈从局部技能执行转移到维护任务前沿一致性，任务状态不对齐导致无依据交接、阶段锁定等失败。

Method: 提出可检查对齐框架ContextFlow，将阶段表示为显式契约，运行时观测转化为证据包，并应用继续、细化、转移、提升和修复等范围更新。

Result: 实验和演示轨迹表明基于证据的范围更新能诊断和缓解重复出现的任务状态失败。

Conclusion: ContextFlow有效提升长时程具身任务中任务前沿对齐的显式性和可审计性，减少一致性失败。

中文摘要：长时程具身代理越来越多地将导航、搜索、接近和操作委托给专门执行器。随着这些执行器变得更强，主要瓶颈从局部技能执行转移到在规划、监控、记忆和执行之间维护一致的任务前沿。我们研究了任务状态不对齐，这是一种任务级一致性失败，其中规划器的活动阶段、运行时证据、记忆上下文和委托执行器不再支持相同的下一步决策。这种失败可能导致无依据的交接、阶段锁定、执行器上下文不匹配以及不必要的重新规划。我们提出了ContextFlow，一个可检查的对齐框架，将阶段表示为显式契约，将运行时观测转换为证据包，并应用范围更新，包括继续、细化、转移、提升和修复。ContextFlow保持专门执行器负责局部闭环控制，同时使任务前沿对齐显式且可审计。在长时程具身任务上的实验和演示轨迹说明了基于证据的范围更新如何诊断和缓解重复出现的任务状态失败。

Original abstract: Long-horizon embodied agents increasingly delegate navigation, search, approach, and manipulation to specialist executors. As these executors become stronger, the main bottleneck shifts from local skill execution to maintaining a coherent task frontier across planning, monitoring, memory, and execution. We study task-state misalignment, a task-level consistency failure in which the planner's active stage, runtime evidence, remembered context, and delegated executor no longer justify the same next-step decision. This failure can lead to unsupported handoffs, stage lock, executor-context mismatch, and unnecessary replanning. We propose ContextFlow, an inspectable alignment framework that represents stages as explicit contracts, converts runtime observations into evidence packets, and applies scoped updates including continue, refine, transfer, promote, and repair. ContextFlow keeps specialist executors responsible for local closed-loop control while making task-frontier alignment explicit and auditable. Experiments and demonstration traces on long-horizon embodied tasks illustrate how evidence-grounded scoped updates diagnose and mitigate recurring task-state failures.

</details>

### [104] [Protein Thoughts: Interpretable Reasoning with Tree of Thoughts and Embedding-Space Flow Matching for Protein-Protein Interaction Discovery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21522v1)
*Kingsley Yeon,Xuefeng Liu,Promit Ghosal*

Main category: q-bio.QM

Selection reason: Tree-of-Thoughts用于蛋白质发现，可迁移至代码优化agent

TL;DR: Protein Thoughts通过将PPI发现转化为可解释搜索问题，结合多种生物学信号和假设引导的熵正则化思维树搜索，在SHS148k上取得排名76%提升和Micro-F1 91.08的优异性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有PPI预测方法只给出排序结果，缺乏机制性解释，导致生物学家无法判断预测是否可信，阻碍了实际应用。

Method: 提出Protein Thoughts框架：将结合证据分解为序列相似性、结构互补性、界面平衡性和化学相容性四个可解释信号，通过透明价值函数保留各自贡献；采用假设引导的熵正则化思维树搜索，由微调语言模型生成搜索指令，结合玻尔兹曼策略平衡利用与探索，并通过假设感知剪枝和假设条件化嵌入空间流匹配处理不确定候选。

Result: 在SHS148k基准上，平均最佳结合子排名11.2（基线47.7，提升76%），结合预测Micro-F1达91.08±0.19，优于现有PPI方法。

Conclusion: Protein Thoughts通过可解释性和高性能证明了其有效性，为PPI发现提供了可信的框架。

中文摘要：蛋白质-蛋白质相互作用（PPI）几乎支配着所有细胞过程，然而用于识别结合伴侣的计算方法通常会产生排序预测，而缺乏机制性解释。这造成了采纳的根本障碍，因为生物学家无法评估预测是否反映了真正的生化见解还是虚假的相关性。我们提出了Protein Thoughts，一个将PPI发现重新表述为具有显式推理的可解释搜索问题的框架。该系统将结合证据分解为四个具有生物学意义的信号：反映进化关系的序列相似性、捕获几何互补性的结构互补性、界面平衡性以及编码残基级别相互作用的化学相容性。我们没有将这些信号合并成一个不透明的分数，而是通过一个透明的价值函数保留它们各自的贡献，从而实现排序和审计。为了高效地导航大型候选空间，我们引入了假设引导的熵正则化思维树搜索。一个微调的语言模型从嵌入衍生特征生成搜索指令，将候选分类为高优先级、探索性或可跳过。这些指令条件化一个玻尔兹曼策略，该策略平衡利用与熵驱动的探索，同时假设感知剪枝防止过早放弃有希望的候选。对于表现出分数不一致的候选，假设条件化的嵌入空间流匹配将蛋白质嵌入向结合子流形传输。在SHS148k基准测试上，Protein Thoughts实现了平均最佳结合子排名11.2，而熵树搜索基线为47.7，提升了76%，对于结合预测，训练的价值函数达到了91.08 ± 0.19的Micro-F1，优于同一数据集上的现有PPI方法。

Original abstract: Protein-protein interactions (PPIs) govern nearly all cellular processes, yet computational methods for identifying binding partners typically produce ranked predictions without mechanistic justification. This creates a fundamental barrier to adoption because biologists cannot assess whether predictions reflect genuine biochemical insight or spurious correlations. We present \textbf{Protein Thoughts}, a framework that reformulates PPI discovery as an interpretable search problem with explicit reasoning. The system decomposes binding evidence into four biologically meaningful signals: sequence similarity reflecting evolutionary relationships, structural complementarity capturing geometric fit, interface balance, and chemical compatibility encoding residue-level interactions. Rather than collapsing these signals into an opaque score, we preserve their individual contributions through a transparent value function that enables both ranking and auditing. To navigate large candidate spaces efficiently, we introduce hypothesis-guided entropy-regularized Tree-of-Thoughts search. A fine-tuned language model generates search directives from embedding-derived features, classifying candidates as high-priority, exploratory, or skippable. These directives condition a Boltzmann policy that balances exploitation with entropy-driven exploration, while hypothesis-aware pruning prevents premature abandonment of promising candidates. For candidates exhibiting score disagreement, hypothesis-conditioned embedding-space flow matching transports protein embeddings toward the binder manifold. On the SHS148k benchmark, Protein Thoughts achieves mean best-binder rank of 11.2 versus 47.7 for an entropic tree search baseline, a 76% improvement, and for binding prediction the trained value function achieves $91.08 \pm 0.19$ Micro-F1, outperforming existing PPI methods on the same dataset.

</details>
